Srinivasamakhi Vedantadesika: Dasavidhahetunirupana (part of the Vaikhanasasutratatparyacintamani)
Based on (pp. 1-122) the of the Devanāgarī-ed. by R. Parthasarathi Bhattacarya:
Śrīvaikhānasagṛhyasūtra (= DHN[D]); 2 vols., Akulamannāḍu, 1967 (reprint Tirupati, 1997/98).

FURTHER NOTES BY THE CONTRIBUTOR:
Die in eckige Klammern gesetzten Angaben im Text sowie die Anmerkungen sind Ergänzungen von Ute Hüsken.
Die Angaben aus dem Inhaltsverzeichnis der Devanāgarī-Edition sind in eckigen Klammern als Zwischenüberschriften in den Text eingefügt.
Die Quellennachweise bei Zitaten stehen in eckigen Klammern am rechten Rand oder in den Anmerkungen - dort ohne eckige Klammern.
Abweichende Lesarten der älteren Telugu-Ausgabe des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa (Abk.: DHN[T]; s.u.) sowie der zitierten Texte sind gelegentlich in Anmerkungen notiert, jedoch nicht durchgängig.*{1}*

Wird im Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa durch kurze Zitate auf längere Textzusammenhänge Bezug genommen, sind diese - sofern verifiziert - an der ersten Stelle ihres Vorkommens vollständig in den Anmerkungen zitiert. An weiteren Stellen wird auf das erste Zitat verwiesen. Die Verse sind in der vorliegenden Textwiedergabe der Ausgabe folgend eingerückt, Daṇḍas im Prosa-Text durch Punkte und Kommata ersetzt.

Das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa liegt in zwei Editionen vor,*{2}* die beide von dem Vaikhānasa-Gelehrten Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya besorgt wurden. Die erste Edition erschien 1931 in Telugu-Schrift und umfaßt als Grundtext nur das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa.
Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa by Śrīnivāsa Dīkṣita [in Telugu-script], ed. as Śrīvaikhānasasūtratātparyacintāmaṇidhṛto Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇākhyo bhāgaḥ, with Sanskrit-commentary and explanations in Telugu by Rompicarla Bhattar Srinivasa Aiyangar, Igavaripalem, 1931 (Śrīvaikhānasagranthamālā, Anubandha 5).

Wenngleich dieser Telugu-Druck an vielen Stellen die vermutlich richtigere Lesart enthält und die darin gegebenen Zitate den zitierten Texten in der uns heute gedruckt vorliegenden Form häufig näherkommen, ist der Textwiedergabe in der vorliegenden Arbeit die 36 Jahre später erschienene Devanāgarī-Edition zugrunde gelegt, da der Telugu-Druck an vielen Stellen nicht mehr lesbar ist. Zudem ist die ältere Telugu-Edition des Textes weltweit nur in wenigen Bibliotheken vorhanden und wegen der Brüchigkeit des Papiers kaum zu benutzen. Selbst im vorbildlich restaurierten Exemplar der Niedersächsischen Staats-und Universitätsbibliothek Göttingen (Signatur A 2000 A 35512) sind etliche Passagen unleserlich. Der Edition von 1931 in Telugu-Schrift ist neben dem Text des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa auch der Sanskrit-Kommentar Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇavyākhyāna (Abk.: DHNV) und eine Telugu-Erläuterung des Herausgebers beigegeben. Zudem enthält das Werk noch einen Zitatindex von 13 Seiten, so daß das Buch insgesamt stattliche 748 Druckseiten umfaßt. Der Umfang des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇavyākhyāna übertrifft dabei den des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa selbst bei weitem. Im Vorwort dieser Ausgabe äußert der Herausgeber sich nicht zu den der Edition zugrunde liegenden Manuskripten.
In der zweiten Edition von 1967 gab Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa zusammen mit dem Tātparyacintāmaṇi in zwei Bänden in Devanāgarī-Schrift heraus. Der Text dieser Ausgabe umfaßt 122 Druckseiten. Im Vorwort gibt Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya zu den dabei benutzten Manuskripten lediglich an, daß sie ihm sämtlich von Vaikhānasa-Familien zur Verfügung gestellt worden seien, und daß alle Manuskripte hinsichtlich der Fehler und Auslassungen identisch seien ("Introduction", S. v). Es ist davon auszugehen, daß er für diese Edition mindestens drei Handschriften konsultierte, die ihm drei Personen aus Andhra Pradesh (Ākuḷamannāḍu, Tirupati, Nallūru) überließen ("Introduction", S. viii). Da Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya seine Telugu-Edition des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa von 1931 mit keinem Wort erwähnt, bleibt unklar, ob er ganz andere Manuskripte verwendete oder ob die textliche Basis beider Editionen identisch ist.

-----
!{1}! Besonderheiten des Telugu-Textes, die den Gepflogenheiten alter Telugu-Drucke entsprechen, sind nicht gesondert vermerkt (s. dazu Grünendahl, 2001, S. xviiff.). Auf abweichende Lesarten im Telugu-Druck weist die Abkürzung "DHN[T]" mit Seitenzahl, aber ohne Zeilenangabe hin. Diese Unterscheide zwischen Devanāgarī- und Telugu-Ausgabe sind allerdings hier noch nicht vollständig erfaßt
!{2}! In keiner der beiden Editionen sind Lesarten angegeben.

Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa

[maṅgalācaraṇam]

[1.1] śrīmadvikhanasa mahāgurave namaḥ /
[1.2] śrī śrīnivāsa parabrahmaṇe namaḥ //

[1.3-4] śrī śrīnivāsamakhikṛte śrīvaikhānasagṛhyasūtratātparyacintāmaṇau daśavidhahetunirūpaṇam
[1.5] vaikhānasakulodbhūtaṃ veṅkaṭeśārcanāratam*{3}* /
[1.6] vedāntadeśikaṃ vande śrīnivāsāryadīkṣitam //

[1.7] śrīveṅkaṭeśam akhileśam anantam ādyaṃ kāruṇyavāridhim aśeṣasurais suvandyam /
[1.8] vande samastajagatāṃ sthitisṛṣṭihetuṃ mānyān gurūṃś ca śataśo*{4}* bhṛgukaśyapādīn //

[1.9] śrutismṛtinadīpūrṇaṃ śāstrakallolasaṅkulam /
[1.10] viṣṇubhaktyudakaṃ śuddhaṃ vande vaikhānasārṇavam* //{5}*

[1.11] yenānyakḷptasūtrāṇāṃ*{6}* netraṃ nistimirīkṛtam /
[1.12] sūtraṃ vaikhānasaṃ hy etat*{7}* caturvargaphalapradam //

[1.13] śrutismṛtītihāsādyaiḥ pratipāditavaibhavām /
[1.14] paramātmaparāṃ vande sūtropaniṣadaṃ parām //

[vyākhyānakartṛgotranāmādi]

[1.15] śrīmatkauśikavaṃśyena*{8}* govindācāryasūnunā /
[1.16] śrīveṅkaṭeśapādābjasaparyāsu ratātmanā //

[1.17] śrutismṛtipurāṇādisiddhamārgānuvartinā /
[1.18] pūrvācāryaparikṣuṇṇasampradāyānuyāyinā //

[1.19] vedāntācāryavaryeṇa śrīnivāsāryayajvanā /
[1.20] vaikhānasasya sūtrasya vyākhyā samyak prakāśyate //

!{3}! DHN[T] 1: veṅkaṭeśārcanāvaram. !{4}! DHN[T] 2: vaikhānasān munivarān statt mānyān gurūṃś ca śataśo. !{5}! Dieser Vers ist auch zu Beginn der Thanjavur-Edition des Vimānārcanakalpa (S. 3) als "Śrīvikhanasācāryastotrapāṭha" zitiert; dort steht zuvor der Śloka: śrautasmārtakarma nikhilam yena sūtritam / tasmai samasta vedārthavidhe vikhanasa namaḥ. !{6}! DHN[T] 5: sūtrāṇām anyakḷptānāṃ. !{7}! DHN[T] 6: sūtrāṇām uttamaṃ sūtraṃ. !{8}! DHN[T] 9: śrīmatkauśikagotreṇa.

[vikhānasasūtrasya tadanuyāyināṃ ca sarvotkṛṣṭatve daśavidhahetūnāṃ nirdeśaḥ]

[2.1-3] atha satyatvādisamastakalyāṇaguṇaviśiṣṭāt parabrahmaṇaḥ śrīmannārāyaṇād utpannena vikhanaśśabdavācyena caturmukhabrahmaṇā praṇītasya vaikhānasasūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatve tatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭatamatve ca daśavidhahetavo nirūpyante. [2.4] yathā: [2.5-9] akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvāt.*{9}* sarvasūtrāṇām āditvāt.*{10}* sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritvāt.*{11}* samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvāt.*{12}* niṣekasaṃskārādimatvāt.*{13}* aṣṭādaśaśārīrasaṃskārapratipādakatvāt.*{14}* sāṅgakriyākalāpavattvāt.*{15}* manvādyaiḥ svīkṛtatvāt.*{16}* akhilajagadekakāraṇabhūtaśrīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvāt.*{17}* etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānavatām eva bhagavatpriyatamatvopapatteś ca.*{18}* iti. [2.10-12] ebhir hetubhir asya sūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānād eva vaikhānasānāṃ sarvebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamatvāñ ca śrutismṛtipurāṇādimukhena pratipādyate. tatrādau akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvād iti hetur nirūpyate. [2.13] vikhanaśśabdārthanirṇayaḥ

[nārāyaṇasya vikhano vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvam]

[2.14] vikhanā nāma kaścid ṛṣiḥ, uta nārāyaṇaḥ? nārāyaṇa eva kevalaṃ. [2.15-16] munimātrasya vaikhānasaśabdavācyatvena pratipādanābhāvāt. paramātmano nārāyaṇasya vikhano vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣv avagamyate. yathā: [2.17] khilaśrutau: "dhenur vahāṇām aditis surāṇāṃ brahmā ṛbhūṇāṃ vikhanā munīnām".

[2.18-19] iti śruyate. ayam arthaḥ. vahānāṃ ataḍudādīnāṃ dhenuḥ utpattikāraṇam. surāṇāṃ indrādīnām aditiḥ. ṛbhūṇāṃ:
[2.20] "sādhyā viśve ca vasavo maruto ṛbhavas tathā /
[2.21] tathaivāṅgiraso rudrā ādityāś ca tathaiva ca /
[2.22] ete devagaṇāś cāṣṭau manvantaragaṇeśvarāḥ //"

[2.23] iti bhṛgūktānāṃ sādhyādīnāṃ brahmā. munīnāṃ muniśabdavācyānāṃ vikhanāḥ.

[2.24] brahmaṇo muniśabdavācyatvaṃ bhārate cāvagamyate

[2.25] "niśāṃ suptvātha bhagavān kṣapānte pratyabuddhyata* /{19}* [MBh 13, App. 3.265]

!{9}! Hetu 1; s. DHN[D] 29.16-70.16. !{10}! Hetu 2; s. DHN[D] 71.1-72.22. !{11}! Hetu 3; s. DHN[D] 73.1-76.21. !{12}! Hetu 4; s. DHN[D] 77.1-79.8. !{13}! Hetu 5; s. DHN[D] 80.1-85.25. !{14}! Hetu 6; s. DHN[D] 86.1-89.16. !{15}! Hetu 7; s. DHN[D] 90.1-91.24. !{16}! Hetu 8; s. DHN[D] 92.1-94.21. !{17}! Hetu 9; s. DHN[D] 95.1-117.10. !{18}! Hetu 10; s. DHN[D] 118.1-122.14. !{19}! MBh: niśā supto 'tha bhagavān.

[3.1] paścād buddhvā sasarjāpaḥ tāsu vīryam avāsṛjat* //{20}* [MBh 13, App. 3.266]

[3.2] tad aṇḍam abhavad dhaimaṃ sahasrāṃśusamaprabham / [MBh 13, App. 3.267]

[3.3] ahaṅkṛtyā*{21}* tatas tasmin sasarja prabhur īśvaraḥ / [MBh 13, App. 3.268]

[3.4] hiraṇyagarbhaṃ viśvātmā brahmāṇaṃ jalajaṃ*{22}* munim //" iti [MBh 13, App. 3.269]

[3.5] aṇḍabahutvābhiprāyeṇa munīnām iti bahuvacanam. yathā

[3.6] "aṇḍānān tu sahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇy ayutāni ca /

[3.7] īdṛśānām anantānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ce//"ti smaraṇāt.

[3.8] niśā cātra pralayaḥ, sā etāvatīti kutrāvagamyata iti cet.

[3.9] mahābhārate: "caturyugasahasrāṇi caturyugaśatāni ca*{23}* / [MBh 13, App. 3.261]

[3.10] prāhuḥ kalpasahasran tu*{24}* brāhmaṇās tattvadarśinaḥ / [MBh 13, App. 3.262]

[3.11] daśakalpasahasrāṇi apy ayas sā mahāniśā*{25}* //" iti. [MBh 13, App. 3.263]

[3.12-13] anayā khilaśrutyā bhagavato vikhanaśśabdavācyatvaṃ katham avagamyata iti cet ucyate.

[itihāsapurāṇābhyām eva vedārthasya nirṇeyatvam]

[3.14] "durbodhā vaidikāś śabdā prakīrṇatvāc ca ye khilāḥ /
[3.15] tadjñais ta eva spaṣṭārthāḥ smṛtitantre pratiṣṭhitāḥ //"*{26}* iti

[3.16] "yadi vidyāc caturvedān sāṅgopaniṣadān dvijaḥ /
[3.17] na cet purāṇasadvidyā na vedārthavicakṣaṇaḥ //" iti

[3.18] "itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛhmayet*{27}* /
[3.19] bibhety alpaśruvād*{28}* vedo mām ayaṃ pratariṣyati //" iti ca [MBh 1.1.204]

[3.20-21] smaraṇāt itihāsapurāṇābhyām evārthanirṇayaḥ kartavyaḥ. bhārate mokṣadharme nāradastutau:

[3.24] tatraiva: "yat tasminn upalabhyaṃ te tat tejas tat trayīmayam /

Bezug auf MahāU 1.1: athāto mahopaniṣadaṃ vyākhyāsyāmas tad āhur eko ha vai nārāyaṇa āsīn na brahmā neśāno nāpo nāgniśomau neme dyāvāpṛthivī na nakṣatrāṇi na sūryo na candramāḥ. sa ekākī na ramate. tasya dhyānāntaḥsthasya yajñastomam ucyate. tasmin puruṣāś caturdaśa jāyante. ekā kanyā. daśendriyāṇi mana ekādaśaṃ tejaḥ. dvādaśam ahaṅkāraḥ. trayodaśaḥ prāṇāḥ. caturdaśaḥ ātmā. pañcadaśī buddhiḥ. bhūtāni pañca tanmātrāṇi. pañca mahābhūtāni. sa ekaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ puruṣaḥ. tatpuruṣam puruṣo niveśya nāsya pradhānasaṃvatsarā jāyante. saṃvatsarādadhijāyante. atha punar eva nārāyaṇaḥ so 'nyatkāmo manasādhyāyata. tasya dhyānāntaḥsthasya lalāṭān trayakṣaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ puruṣo jāyate. bibhrac chriyaṃ yaśaḥ satyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ tapo vairāṅyaṃ mana aiśvaryaṃ sapraṇava vyāhṛtaya ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvāṅgirasaḥ sarvāṇi chandāṃsi tāny aṅge samāśritāni. tasmād īśāno mahādevo mahād eva. atha punar eva nārāyaṇaḥ so 'nyatkāmo manasādhyāyata. tasya dhyānāntaḥsthasya lalāṭāt svedo 'patat. tā imāḥ pratatā āpaḥ tatas tejo hiraṇyamayam aṇḍam. tatra brahmā caturmukho 'jāyata. Lies mit DHN[T] 88: viriñcaṃ. !{69}! DHN[T] 88 ins. (śatānandaś śatadhṛtir vikhanāś ca viriñcanaḥ). !{70}! Lies mit DHN[T] 88: caturmukha. !{71}! DHN[T] 88: itīrita. !{72}! DHN[T] 89: atra kārya kāraṇayor abhede(datve?)nāvagamāt. !{73}! DHN[T] 89: vaikhānasādiśabdaprayogaprakāraḥ. !{74}! DHN[T] 91: vaikhānasānām utpattiḥ (śrutau). !{75}! DHN[T] 91: (śrūyate). !{76}! TĀ: āsant. !{77}! Bezug auf TĀ 1.23.1: āpo vā idam āsant salilam eva. sa prajāpatir ekaḥ puṣkaraparṇe samabhavat. tasāntar manasi kāmaḥ samavartata. idaṃ sṛjeyam iti. tasmād yat puruṣo manasābhigacchati. tadvācā vadati. tat karmaṇā karoti. tad eṣābhyanūktā. kāmas tadagre samavartatadhi. manaso retaḥ prathamaṃ yad āsīt. S.a. DHN[D] 6.22. !{78}! Bezug auf TĀ 1.23.2: sato bandhum asati niravindan. hṛdi prītiṣyā kavayo manoṣeti. upainaṃ tad upanamati. yat kāmo bhavati. ya evaṃ veda. sa tapo 'tapyata. sa tapas taptvā. śarīram adhūnuta. tasya yan māṃsam āsīt. tato 'ruṇāḥ ketavo vātaraśanā ṛṣaya udatiṣṭhan. !{79}! Bezug auf TĀ 1.23.3: ye nakhāḥ. te vaikhānasāḥ. ye bālāḥ. te vālakhilyāḥ. yo rasaḥ. so 'pāṃ. antarataḥ kūrmaṃ bhūtaṃ sarpanraṃ. tam abravīt. mama vai tvaṅmāṃsā. samabhūt. !{80}! DHN[T] 92 om. caturmukhaḥ. !{81}! DHN[T] 92: matsyāvatārādirūpeṇāvatariṣyamāṇasya. !{82}! DHN[T] 92: sampratipannaśrīvaikhānasaśāstramārgeṇa. !{83}! Lies: dhyānenānukṛtavān; DHN[T] 93: dhyānenānu(bhavaṃ)kṛtavān (caturmukhaḥ).

[sanakādisṛṣṭiprakāraḥ]

[9.1-5] ity ārabhya*{84}* brahmaṇā brahuśaḥ*{85}* kṛtaṃ tapaścaraṇam uktam. tapaścaraṇakāle sākṣātkṛtabhagavatsvarūpavaibhavānubhavātiśayāt bhagavaddattasṛṣṭiśaktilābhāt tadupajanitaviśeṣavegāc ca pulakitasarvāṅgaḥ śarīram adhūnuta - kampam akarot. "tasya yan māṃsam āsīd"*{86}* māṃsaṃ mānasam iti yāvat. "arthāt prakaraṇāl liṅgād aucityād arthanirṇayaḥ" ity arthādibhiḥ*{87}* samīcīnārthanirṇayavidhānāt "akṣarasāmyān nirbrūyād"*{88}* iti niruktavidhānāñ ca.

[9.6-10] tathā ca tasya manaḥ paramātmani saṃsaktam āsīd iti yat, tena hetunā tadanugrahas samajani. tenānugṛhītāt brahmaṇaḥ "ketavo vātaraśanāḥ ṛṣayaḥ udatiṣṭhan"*{89}*. "aruṇāḥ" paramātmani vasantaḥ taditararaviktāḥ "ketavaḥ" ucchritasvabhāvāḥ paramātmapravaṇānām agresarāḥ "vātaraśanā" digvāsasaḥ "ṛṣayaḥ" sarvārthadarśinaḥ sanakādayaḥ "udatiṣṭhan" utkṛṣya samabhavan iti.*{90}*
[9.11] idaṃ viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi: "sanandanādayo ye ca pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭās tu vedhasā /
[9.12] na te lokeṣv asajjanta nirapekṣāḥ prajāvidhau* //{91}* [ViṣṇuP 1.7.9]

[9.13] sarve te yogino jātā*{92}* vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ /
[9.14] teṣv evaṃ nirapekṣeṣu lokasṛṣṭau mahātmanaḥ //" ityādinā pratipāditam.*{93}* [ViṣṇuP 1.7.10]

[9.15-19] sa prajāpatiḥ evaṃvidhān svakāryāsādhakān tān dṛṣṭvā kiñcid viṣādam āpannaḥ punar api svakāraṇaṃ bhagavantaṃ dhyānaprayāyeṇa khananenātoṣat. "ye nakhā" ityādi*{94}*. bhagavadanugrahavikasite prajāpater manasi vaikhānasā nāma ṛṣayas sambhūtāḥ atra "ye nakhā" ity atra ādyantavarṇaviparyayo bhavati. "kaśyapaḥ paśyako bhavatī"tivat "khanā ity etat nakhā" iti viparyastam iti yāvat.*{95}*
[9.20] "suptiṅupagrahaliṅganarāṇāṃ kālahalacsvarakartṛyaṅañ*{96}* ca /
[9.21] vyatyayam icchiti*{97}* śāstrakṛd eṣāṃ so 'pi ca siddhyati bāhulakena //"

[9.22-24] iti, "bahulaṃ chandasī"*{98}*ti cātra praṇāman*{99}*. atra "anakhā" iti cchittvā kecid evam ūcuḥ*{100}*. anakhā ity anena saumyendriyavatvaṃ uktam iti*{101}*.

!{84}! DHN[T] 93 ins. "śūdrajātiṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ paśūnām aśvam eva" cetyantaṃ (evaṃ?). !{85}! Lies mit DHN[T] 93: bahuśaḥ. !{86}! Bezug auf TĀ 1.23.3; s. DHN[D] 8.15-19. !{87}! DHN[T] 94: arthanirṇaya" arthanirṇaye vidhānāt. !{88}! Bezug auf Nirukta 2.1: avidyamāne sāmānye apy akṣaravarṇasāmānyān nirbrūyān na tv eva na nirbrūyāt. !{89}! Bezug auf TĀ 1.23.2; s. DHN[D] 8.15-19. !{90}! DHN[T] 95 statt 9.6-10: tathā tasya manaḥ paramātmani saṃsaktam āsīd iti yat, tena hetunā tadanugrahas samajani. tenānugṛhītā brāhmaṇāḥ (tāt brahmaṇaḥ) aruṇāḥ ketavo vātaraśanā ṛṣaya udatiṣṭhan. yad vā paramātmani vasanta(s sanda)s taditaraviraktāḥ ketava ivocchritasvabhāvāḥ paramātmapravaṇānām agresarāḥ vātaraśanā digvāsasaḥ (sarvārthadarśinaḥ) sanakādaya udatiṣṭhan utkṛṣya samabhavan. !{91}! ViṣṇuP: nirapekṣāḥ prajāsu te. !{92}! ViṣṇuP: sarve te 'bhyāgatajñānā. !{93}! DHN[T] 95: mahātmana" iti. !{94}! Bezug auf TĀ 1.23.3; s. DHN[D] 8.15-19. !{95}! DHN[T] 96 statt DHN[D] 9.15-19: sa prajāpatir evaṃvi(dhānyannādau)dhas svakāryāsādhakāṃ dṛṣṭvā kiñcid viṣādam āpannaḥ punar api svakāraṇaṃ bhagavantaṃ dhyānaparyāyanāma khananenātoṣayat. "ye nakhā" iti bhagavadanugrahavikasite prajāpater manasi vaikhānasā nāma ṛṣayas sambhūtāḥ ye nakhā ity atrādyantavarṇaviparyayo bhavati. kaśyapaḥ >>>paśyako bhavatī"tivat. !{96}! DHN[T] 96: kālahalacsvarakartṛyaṅāṃ. !{97}! Lies: icchati. !{98}! Aṣṭadhyāyī 2.3.62, 2.4.39, 73 und 76. !{99}! DHN[T] 96: ca statt cātra praṇāman. !{100}! Anm. des Herausgebers: na vidyante khāni indriyāṇi yeṣāṃ te nakhāḥ. na nakhāḥ anakhāḥ nañdvayena saumyendrayavatvaṃ phalitam. !{101}! DHN[T] 97: "anakhā" ityatra cchittvā kecid evam ūcuḥ. anakhā ity anena sarve(saumye)ndriyavatvaṃ uktam syād iti.

[vaikhānasānām ācāryapuruṣatvam]

[10.1-3] evañ ca sati "saumyaṃ jitendriyaṃ"*{102}* "suprasannendriyaṃ"*{103}* ityādinā bhagavacchāstreṣv ācāryalakṣaṇasya*{104}* pratipāditatvāt "vaikhānasa vikhanasācarya"*{105}* iti. viṣṇor*{106}* ācāryatvena śāntyparvaṇy abhihitatvāt.

[10.14] "yeṣāṃ trīṇy avadātāni yonirvidyā ca karma ca /

[10.23] loke vihartum icchāmi yad ahaṃ*{118}* padmasambhava /

[12.18] taṃ hareḥ purataḥ kṛtvā proktavān kamalāsanaḥ // [ĀS 4.28]

[12.19] brahmovāca: devadeva jagannātha sṛṣṭisthityantakāraṇa /
[12.20] bhagavaṃs tvatprabhāvena sṛṣṭo 'yaṃ munisattamaḥ* //{147}* [ĀS 4.29]

[12.21] jātāḥ cintayato mattas tvat sṛṣṭau munayas tv ime /
[12.22] etair api kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ jagad etac carācaraṃ // [ĀS 4.30]

[12.23] matputrāṇāṃ ca sarveṣām agrajaḥ puruṣottamaḥ /
[12.24] vaiṣṇaveṣv agrajaś śreṣṭho munīnāṃ prathamo muniḥ // [Ā.S 4.31]

!{136}! ĀS: sanatkumāraś ca tathā sanakaś ca sanātanaḥ / sanandana iti khyātā brahmavidyāviśāradāḥ; so liest auch DHN[T] 104. !{137}! ĀS: sanmuniśreṣṭhā. !{138}! [19.7-10] "ye vālāḥ te vālakhilyāḥ" ity atra bakārasthāne vakāra*{211}*. jñānātiśayavaibhavāt kāmādidoṣarāhityena ca bālā ucyante. śrūyate hi*{212}*: "tasmād brāhmaṇaḥ pāṇḍityaṃ nirvidya bālyena tiṣṭhāset*{213}* bālyañ ca pāṇdityañ ca nirvidyātha muniḥ" iti.

[19.11-13] atra kecid evam ūcuḥ: brahmaṇaḥ vidhūtāc charīrāt yanmāṃsaṃ vikīrṇam abhavat tato ketavo vātaraśanā ṛṣaya udatiṣṭhann iti. tad asat. evam arthasvīkāre sṛṣṭikāraṇabhūtasya brahmaśarīrasya śaithilyam uktaṃ syād iti.

[19.14-20] kiñ ca "tasyāntarmanasi kāmas samavartata" ityādinā "kāmas tadagre samavartatādhi" ity antena sopapattikaṃ vartamānaṃ saṅkalparūpaṃ mananavyāpāram uktvā "manaso retaḥ prathamaṃ yad āsīd" ity atra tatra vidyamānasya vyāpārasya prajāpateḥ sṛṣṭikāraṇatvaṃ retaś śabdebis hier telugunoktvā "sato bandhum asati niravindann" ity ārabhya "ya evaṃ veda" ity antena brahmaṇas tatkālavidyamānamānasaśaktimāab hier telugutreṇa vyaṣṭisṛṣṭer aniṣpannatvam uktvā manaso vyaṣṭikāraṇalābhāya "sa tapo 'tapyata" iti bhagavadupāsanam akarod" ity uktam. ayam evārthaḥ "oṃ ity ekākṣaraṃ brahme"tyādinā brahmāṇḍe 'py uktam.*{214}*

[23.16] vaikhānasāḥ kathaṃ brūyuḥ kathaṃ vā pāñcarātrikāḥ // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1653]

[23.18] sthaṇḍile padmakaṃ kṛtvā sāṣṭapatraṃ*{243}* sakarṇikam // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1655]

[23.20] vaidikair athavā mantrair mama sūktena vā punaḥ // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1657]

[23.21] sthitaṃ māṃ mantratas tasmin arcayet susamahitaḥ*{245}* / [MBh 14, App. 4.1658]

[23.22] viṣṇuñ ca puruṣaṃ satyam*{246}* acyutañ ca yudhiṣṭhira*{247}* // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1659]

[23.23] aniruddhañ ca māṃ prāhur vaikhānasavido janāḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1660]

[yajurvedasya vaikhānasaśākhātvaprasiddhiḥ]

[41.1-3] sa ca yajurvedaḥ: "bahuśṛṅgaś catus sānuḥ pṛthulo vedaparvataḥ" ity ārabhyoktarītyā vedavyāsarupiṇā bhagavatā yadā vyastaḥ, tataḥ pūrvam ekarūpeṇāvasthitasya tasya vedaparvatasya vaikhānasaśākhātvaprasiddhir āsīd iti pūrvam eva pratipāditam.

[46.1-5] itthaṃ vāsudevādīnāṃ daivikamānuṣabhedena dvaividhyasya, "puruṣaṃ paramapuruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ paraṃ brahmāṇam" ityādinā pratipāditānāṃ caturṇāṃ puruṣādīnāṃ mūrtivibhāgasya ca śrīvaikhānasaśāstre pratipādanāt, etas sarvavibhāgajña eva caturvyūhavibhāgavid ity anenocyate. ācchidrapañcakālajña iti:*{387}*

[46.10-14] "ye pāvayanti dharaṇīṃ" "ijyāmadhye tathāhome" "ye toṣayanty avirataṃ" iti vacanāni, sāmanyena pañcakālaparāyaṇasya darśanasparśanādibhis sarveṣāṃ pāvanatāṃ kṛtārthatāṃ, ijyāyogādisamayeṣu cāgatasya tasya pūjanāntaraṃ śeṣakarmācaraṇañ ca pratipādayanti, etādṛśaḥ pañcakālaparāyaṇaḥ kīdṛśā ity ākaṅkṣāyāṃ "dvādaśākṣaratattvajña" ityādinā "acchidrapañcakālajña" ity antena tallakṣaṇam ucyate.

[47.13-19] kiñca tatsūtreṣu dvādaśākṣaratattvādipratipādanam api nāsti. evaṃ "sati kuḍye citrakarme"ti nyāyena yajñopavītadhāraṇasandhyopāsanabhagavadārādhanādividhipratipādanarahitasūtrāntaraniṣṭhānāṃ, tathā śrīmannārāyaṇasya samānatvena rudrādidevatāntarārādhanavidhipratipādakasūtraniṣṭhānāñ ca caturvyūhavibhāgajñānāsambhavāt bhagavadārādhanasvarūpajñānābhāvena pañcakālaparāyaṇatvādigandhaleśo 'pi na sambhavati. sūtrāntaroktamārgeṇa vā pañcarātroktamārgeṇa vā bhagavadārādhanaṃ kurvato 'nadhikāriṇo devalakatvaṃ pratipādyate.*{397}*

[pāñcarātre durgādidevatāntarārcanapratipādanam]

[47.22] yo 'sau nārayaṇas*{398}* sākṣāt sa hi vighneśa ucyate* //{399}* [ViṣvaksenaS 10.114]

Lies: nārāyaṇas. !{399}! ViṣvaksenaS: idaṃ tu tava vakṣyāmi guhyād guhyataraṃ mune. !{400}! ViṣvaksenaS: naiva jānanti tadbhedaṃ munayas tatvadarśinaḥ.

[48.1] "kuryāt pāśāṅkuśau vāpi śaṅkhacakrāv athāpi vā* /{401}*

[48.2] ākhuṃ vāpi khagendraṃ vā tasya vāhanam ācaret* //{402}* [ViṣvaksenaS ]

[48.3] nārāyaṇāśakatvāc cāvyāvṛttatvān mahāmune* /{403}*

[48.4] vīśas tadvāhanaṃ proktaṃ ākhuṃ vāpi samācaret // [Viṣvaksena.S ]

[48.5] tasmāc chriyañ ca durgāñ ca vāṇīṃ vighneśam eva ca /
[48.6] svatantreṇārcayed dhīmān sarvakāryārthasiddhaye //" ityādi ca dṛśyate. [ViṣvaksenaS ]

[48.7-10] devatāntarāṇāṃ aṅgabhāvenārcanaṃ na niṣiddhyate. "svatantrabuddhyā kurvan vai brāhmaṇo narakaṃ vrajet" ityādi vacanaiḥ aṅgatvena vinā svātantryeṇāṅgivyatiriktadevatāntarārādhanaṃ niṣiddhyate. tathāvidhaniṣiddhadevatāntarārcanapratipādakaśāstraniṣṭhasya pañcakālaparāyaṇatvaṃ na sambhavati.*{404}*

[paramaikāntinām eva pañcakālaparāyaṇatvam]

[48.11] "yair iṣṭaḥ pañcakālajñair harir ekāntibhir naraiḥ /
[48.12] nūnaṃ tatra mato devo yathā tair vāgudīritaḥ //" ity uktarītyā

[vaikhānasavyatiriktānāṃ paramaikāntitvābhāvaḥ]

[48.13-15] paramaikāntitvāsambhave tad(pañcakālaparāyaṇatvā)sambhavāt. paramaikāntitvañ ca bhagavadekaparatvam eva. tac ca svātantryeṇānyadevatāyājināṃ vaikhānasavyatiriktānāṃ hi na sambhavati.*{405}*
[48.16-17] atra "yair iṣṭaḥ pañcakālajñair" ity anena pañcakālavyatiriktakālāntarapratipādakaśāstraniṣṭhānāṃ*{406}* vyavṛttiḥ. "ekāntibhir narair" ity anena
[48.18] "viprā vaikhānasākhyā ye te bhaktās tattvam ucyate* //{407}* [PauṣkaraS 36.260cd]

[48.19] ekāntinas susattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājinaḥ* //{408}* [PauṣkaraS 36.261ab]

[48.20-23] ityādi pauṣkarasaṃhitāvacanānusāreṇa*{409}* svātantryeṇa durgādidevatāntarārcanapratipādakapāñcarātraśāstraniṣṭhānāṃ*{410}* vyāvṛttiḥ. "nūnam atra mato deva" ity anena - "yatra vaikhānasā viprā yatra santi gavāṃ gaṇāḥ /
[48.24] yatra bilvāḥ palāśāś ca tatra sannihito hariḥ* //{411}*"

[48.25-26] ity asyārtho jñāpyate iti "yair iṣṭa" iti kṛtsnam api vacanaṃ vaikhānasaparam ity evāvagamyate.*{412}*

!{401}! DHN[T] 193: cakraśaṅkhāv; vgl. ViṣvaksenaS 11.294: evaṃ cakrādisaṃproktam aparaṃ cādhunā śṛṇu / dakṣiṇe paraśuṃ nyasya hy adhaḥ pāśāṅkuśaṃ nyaset. !{402}! Vgl. [52.21] nanu:
[52.22] "yo devaṃ pūjayed vipro vittārthī vatsaratrayam /
[52.23] sa vai devalako nāma havyakavyabahiṣkṛtaḥ* //{450}*"

[52.24-53.2] iti devatāpūjakasya devalakatvaṃ sambhavatīti cet - tad asat. sāmānyataḥ devatārādhanaṃ ye kurvanti te devalakā iti vā? uta śrutismṛtītihāsapurāṇādiṣu mukhyādhikāritvena pratipāditā apīti vā?. sāmānyataḥ devatārādhanaṃ ye kurvanti te iti cet - tarhi gṛhadevatāpūjakānām api devalakatvaprasaṅgaḥ. kiñca:*{451}*

!{443}! DHN[T] 201 om. ācamanasya mahāniśāyāṃ niṣedhāt. !{444}! DHN[T] 201: yogasyāyuktatvāt. yogakālasya vyavahitatvāt tatrāpi chidrapāñcakālikatvāt. !{445}! DHN[T] 201 statt DHN[D] 52.5-6: kālacatuṣṭaye 'bhigamanādiṣv ekasya lopasambhavād aniyamitacchidrapañcakālaparasya pāñcakālikasya parāyaṇaśabdā(bhilāpā)sambhavāt. !{446}! DHN[T] 201 führt diesen Vers erst einige Sätze später an (s.u.). !{447}! DHN[T] 201: sāyaṅkālaparyantānām eva (kālānāṃ) ācaraṇakālatvena pratitatvāt. (yathā): hier wird der Śloka, der mit kliśyantīha beginnt, in DHN[T] 201 angeführt. !{448}! Lies: arhantīti. !{449}! DHN[T] 202 statt DHN[D] 52.16-20: ti snānāt pūrvaṃ tattvasṛṣṭer ayuktatvāt. pretaprāyasya saṃhṛtatattvasya svāpayogyatāsambhavāt. "abbhakṣo vāyubhakṣa" ityādi śabdāvadavadhāraṇagarbhasya pāñcakālika(pañcakāla)śabdasya ... aniyamitaparimita pāñcakālikeṣu pāñcarātrikeṣu saṃbhavayogyatābhāvāc cāniyataparimitaviṣam acchidrapāñcakālikāḥ pāñcarātriṇo niyatāchidrapañcakālaparāyaṇo vaikhānaso iti (ca) siddham. !{450}! DHN[T] 234: havyakavyabahiṣkṛta; Kane, HD 2.1, S. 109, Anm. 232, gibt an, daß dies ein Zitat von Devala in Smṛticandrikā II (S. 396) und bei Aparārka (S. 450 und 923) sei. Dort liest er allerdings: devārcanaparo vipro vittārthī vatsaratrayam / asau devalako nāma havyakavyeṣu garhitaḥ //. Vgl. Colas, 1996, S. 135, Anm. 2. Dieser Vers wird im Text Devalakanirṇaya einem Gautama zugeschrieben. !{451}! DHN[T] 234 statt DHN[D] 52.24-53.2: iti devatāpūjakasya devalakatvaṃ sambhavatīti cet - tad asat. sāmānyatvena devatārādhanaṃ ye kurvanti te devalako iti vā? uta śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇādiṣu mukhyādhikāritvena pratipāditāḥ. sāmānyatvena kurvantīti cet - tarhi gṛhadevatāpūjakānām api devalakatvaprasaṅgaḥ. kiñca.

[vaikhānasānām devalakatvābhāvaḥ]

[53.3] "brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vipro vaikhānasas tathā* /{452}*

[53.4] kurvanti*{453}* nijakarmāṇi viṣṇum eva yajanti te //"

[53.5-11] iti sandhyopāsanādīnāṃ bhagavadārādhanarūpatvoktyā*{454}* teṣāñ ca tyāgas sambhavati. atas sāmānyataḥ iti*{455}* vaktum ayuktam. śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu*{456}* mukhyādhikāritvena pratipāditā devalakāḥ*{457}* iti cet - tad asat. "'agnir vai devānām avamo viṣṇuḥ paramas tadantareṇa sarvā anyā devatā'; iti brāhmaṇam. tasmād gṛhe paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sāyaṃ prātar homānte 'rcayati" iti vaikhānasasūtre*{458}*, "pravaḥ pāntam andhaso dhiyāyate maheśūrāya viṣṇave cārcata"*{459}* iti ṛgbrāhmaṇam anusṛtya*{460}* viṣṇupradhānatayā "sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmā" ityādiśrutyuktaviṣṇvādipañcamūrtīnām*{461}* ārādhanasya pratipāditatvāt*{462}*.

[53.12-13] āśvamedhike "kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo 'sī"*{463}*tyādeḥ, vṛddhamanau "vedāntavedibhir"*{464}* ityādeś coktatvāt.

[53.14-15] evam eva pāñcarātraśaivaśilpajyautiṣādiṣu utkṛṣṭamukhyādhikāripratipādakānāṃ vacanānāṃ vaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt tanmūlabhūtaśrutismṛtipurāṇādīnām aprāmāṇyaprasaṅgo duṣpariharaḥ.*{465}*

[vaikhānasānām bhagavaddravyopabhogādau doṣābhāvaḥ]

[53.16-17] evaṃ ca pramāṇabhūteṣu śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu pratipāditānām ācārādīnāṃ tyāgaḥ prasajyet, niṣphalatvāt. nanu paradravyoṇālayārcanaṃ*{466}* kurvatāṃ devalakatvam iti cet na.*{467}*

[53.18-19] śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu tattacchāstreṣu ca ālayārcakānāṃ*{468}* mukhyādhikāritvena taddravyopabhogārhatvena ca pratipādanāt.*{469}*

[53.20] yathā - marīciproktāyām ānandasaṃhitāyāṃ vikhanasotpattyādikaṃ pratipādya:
[53.21] "tathā tvadanujīvitve tvaddravyānubhave sati /
[53.22] yad bhaved doṣa utpanna iti cintākulo 'smy aham* //{470}*" [ĀS 4.77]

[53.23] iti bhagavaddravyopajīvanadoṣabhīroḥ vikhanasaḥ*{471}* bhagavantaṃ prati praśne -

[53.24] "athovāca hṛṣīkeśo bhīruṃ taṃ munisattamaṃ* /{472}* [ĀS 4.78ab]

[53.25] vaikhānasānāṃ tad doṣo nāsti matkṛtakarmaṇām* //{473}* [ĀS 4.83ab]

[54.1] maddravyaṃ havyakavyārthe dānābhyāgatapūjane / [ĀS 4.84cd]

[54.2] mukhyam evāstu bhavatāṃ sadā matkarma kurvatām // [Ā.S 4.85ab]

[vaikhānasānām bhagavadvigrahavikraye 'pi doṣābhāvaḥ]

[54.3] kim ebhir bahubhir vākyair anyat te kathayāmy aham* //{474}* [ĀS 4.85cd]

[54.4] maddravyakṣetrabimbānām ālayānāṃ tathāpadi* /{475}*

[54.5] vikrīṇanādikāryeṣu nāsti doṣo madājñayā* //{476}* [ĀS 4.87]

[54.6] tasmād bhavān abhimatas sarvaṃ karma sadā kuru // [ĀS ]

[54.7] madīyadhanabhogena matkriyālopatas tava /
[54.8] maccharīratayā satyam apacāro na vidyate* //{477}*" [ĀS 4.86]

[54.9] iti bhagavadvacanodāharaṇena bhagavaddravyopabhogādiṣu doṣābhāvaḥ pratipāditaḥ.*{478}*

[54.10-14] atra "ahaṃ bhaktaparādhīno hy asvatantra iva dvija" ityādivacanānusāreṇārcakaparādhīnatāṃ darśayituṃ, bhagavatprītiviṣayīkṛtānāṃ vaikhānasānāṃ taddravyopabhogādiṣu doṣagandho nāstīti pratipādanāvasare "maddravyaṃ kṣetrabimbādī"tyādinā kaimutikanyāyam abhipretya bhagavadvigrahavikraye kṛte 'pi doṣo nāstīty ucyate. tāvatā na tad abhipretam.*{479}*

[54.15-16] nanv evam api devadravyopabhogadoṣas sāmānyataḥ mukhyāmukhyādhikāriṣu sarveṣv āpadyate eva iti cet na.*{480}*

[māṃsabhakṣane narakapatanam]

[54.17] "ye bhakṣayanti māṃsāni sattvānāṃ*{481}* jīvitaiṣiṇām /
[54.18] bhakṣyante te 'pi tais sarvair iti brahmābravīt svayam* //{482}* [MBh 13.117.33]

[54.19] māṃ sa bhakṣayitām utra yasya māṃsam ihādmy aham /
[54.20] etan māṃsasya māṃsatvaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ* //{483}* [MBh 13.117.34]

[54.21] na hi māṃsaṃ tṛṇāt kaṣṭhād upalād vāpi jayate /
[54.22] hatvā jantuṃ bhaven māṃsaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet* //{484}* [MBh 13.116.26]

[54.23] hantā caivānumantā ca viśas tā krayavikrayī /
[54.24] saṃskartā copakartā ca khādakaś cāṣṭa ghātukāḥ* //{485}* [MBh 13.116.47]

!{474}! Vgl. ĀS 16.47ab: kiṃ ebhir bahubhir vākyais satyam eva vadāmy ahaṃ. !{475}! ĀS: maddravyaṃ kṣetrabimbādīn vālayāni yathāpadi; vgl. MBh: māṃ sa bhakṣayate yasmād bhakṣayiṣye tam apy aham / etan māṃsasya māṃsatvam ato budhyasva bhārata. !{484}! MBh: hatvā jantuṃ tato māṃsaṃ tasmād doṣo 'sya bhakṣaṇe. !{485}! [55.1] dhanena krāyako hanti khādakaś copabhogataḥ /
[55.2] ghātuko vadhabandhābhyām ity eṣa trividho vadhaḥ* //{486}* [MBh 13.116.38]

[55.3] svamāṃsaṃ paramāṃsena yo vardhayitum icchati /
[55.4] nāradaḥ prāha dharmātmā narake sa vipacyate* //{487}*" [MBh 13.117.10]

[kutracid dharmasyāpy adharmaṃ, adharmasyāpi dharmatvañ ca]

[55.5-6] ityādi vacanaiḥ māṃsabhakṣaṇena narakapatanasmaraṇāt bhagavatprītyarthaṃ kriyamāṇeṣu yajñeṣv api māṃsabhakṣaṇasattvāt yājñikānām*{488}* api narakapatanaṃ sambhavatīti yāgasyāpi tyāgaprasaṅgāt*{489}*.
[55.7] "tasmāc chāstraṃ pramāṇaṃ te kāryākāryavyavasthitau*{490}* /
[55.8] jñātvā śāstravidhānoktaṃ karma kartum ihārhasi //" [MBh 6.38.24]

[55.9-12] iti bhagavadvacanāt śāstroktānāṃ karmaṇāṃ doṣo nāstīti cet. "maddravyopabhogādau doṣo nāstī"ti bhagavatā pratipāditvāt prakṛte 'pi doṣo nāsty eva. "vacanāt pravṛttir vacanān nivṛttir" iti khalu śiṣṭoktiḥ. evaṃ kutracid dharmo 'dharmaḥ adharmaś ca dharmo bhavati.*{491}*

[55.13] yathā
[55.14] "ukte 'nṛte bhavet kiñcit prāṇināṃ prāṇarakṣaṇam /
[55.15] anṛtaṃ tatra satyaṃ syāt satyam atrānṛtaṃ bhavet //

[55.16] kāminīṣu vivāheṣu gavāṃ*{492}* pīḍāsu bādhane /
[55.17] brāhmaṇābhyavapattau ca śapathe nāsti pātakam //"

[55.18-19] "yadbrāhmaṇaś cābrāhmaṇaś ca praśnam eyātāṃ brāhmaṇāyādhibrūyāt yadbrāhmaṇāyādhyātmane*{493}* 'dhyāha yad brāhmaṇaṃ parāhātmānaṃ parāha tasmād brāhmaṇo na parocyaḥ" ity śrutiś ca.

[55.20-21] śrautasūtre ca: "sarva evam abhivādayanti nābhivādayati na juhoty anyatra somāṅgebhyaḥ" ityādi pratipādyate.*{494}*
[55.22] "sarvasvaharaṇe bhāryāveśyayoḥ (?) prāṇasaṃśaye /
[55.23] godvijārthe vivāde ca śapathe nāsti pātakam //"

[55.24] ityādi smṛtiś ca.*{495}*

[55.25] evaṃ ca śāstroktaprakāreṇa bhagavadarcanaṃ kurvatāṃ taddravyopabhoge*{496}* na doṣaḥ.

[devalakatvalakṣaṇavicāraḥ]

[56.1-2] kiñca - kiṃ devalakatvaṃ jātiparam, uta karmaparam? jātiparam iti vaktuṃ na śakyate. tathānuktatvāt*{497}*. icchayā kalpitum aśakyatvāc ca.*{498}*

[avihitakarmakartṛtvam eva devalakatvam]

[56.3-4] atha karmaparam iti cet. vihitakarmaparam, uta avihitakarmaparam?*{499}* vihitakarmaparam iti vaktum aśakyam - śrutismṛtītihāsasūtrapurāṇādīnām*{500}* apramāṇyaprasaṅgāt.

[56.5] vihitadharmaparatvenānuktatvāt.*{501}*
[56.6] "śrutismṛtī mamaivājñā yas tām ullaṅghya vartate /
[56.7] ājñāc chedī mama drohī madbhakto 'pi na vaiṣṇavaḥ* //{502}*"

[paradravyakṛtasyāpy ārādhanasya nirdoṣatvam]

[56.8] iti bhagavadājñābhaṅgadoṣāc ca. evaṃ ca avihitakarmaparam iti hi pariśiṣyate.*{503}*

[56.9-10] nanu - paradravyeṇa kṛtaṃ bhagavadārādhanaṃ kratuvat parārtham eva bhavatīti cet maivam.*{504}*
[56.11] "anyadharmaparo vipro bhraṣṭo gacchaty adhogatim /
[56.12] matkarmanirato vipro nādhaḥ patati kutracit //"

[56.13] iti bhagavadvacanāt*{505}*.
[56.14] purāṇāntare: "svasminn arpitamātreṇa yena kenāpi karmaṇā /
[56.15] tuṣṭo dadāti svapadam aho vatsalatā*{506}* hareḥ //" iti.

[56.16] kiñca:

[dakṣiṇāpratigrahe doṣābhavaḥ]

[56.17] "ekaviṃśatiniṣkantu dadyād ācāryadakṣiṇām /
[56.18] ṛtvijān tu tadardhaṃ syāt tadardham itarasya ca //"

[56.19] iti dakṣiṇādānaṃ pratipādyate.*{507}*

[56.20] nanu - "pratigraheṇa viprasya brāhmaṃ tejo vinaśyati* //{508}*" iti manuvacanāt*{509}* [ManuDhŚ 4.186cd]

[56.21-25] "pratigraheṇa tejo hi viprāṇāṃ śāmyate" ity ānuśāsanikavacanāc ca pratigraheṇa brahmatejonāśanaṃ smaryate. śrūyate pratigrahe prāyaścittam api. "yo yājayati prati vā gṛhṇāti yājayitvā pratigṛhya vānaśnaṃs tris svādhyāyam adhīyīta trirātraṃ sāvitrīṃ gāyatrīm anvatirecayati varo dakṣiṇā vareṇaiva varaṃ spṛṇoty ātmā hi varaḥ" iti.

[56.25] ataḥ pratigrahe doṣo 'stīti cet - na.*{510}*

!{497}! DHN[T] 242: anuktatvāt. !{498}! DHN[T] 242 ins. (jātiparam na bhavati). !{499}! DHN[T] 242: vihitakarmaparam (vā), utāvihitakarmaparam?. !{500}! DHN[T] 242: śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇādīnām. !{501}! DHN[T] 242: vihitakarmaparatvenānuktatvāt. !{502}! Dieser Vers ist auch in DHN[D] 65.13-14 zitiert. !{503}! DHN[T] 243: iti bhagavadājñābhaṅgadoṣāś ca. DHN[T] 244-245 statt DHN[D] 56.21-25: "pratigraheṇa tejo hi viprāṇāṃ śāmyate" na tu? ity ānuśāsanikavacanāc ca pratigraheṇa brahmatejonāśanaṃ, prāyaścittam api śrūyate. "yo yājayati prati vā gṛhṇāti yājayitvā pratigṛhya vānaśnaṃs tris svādhyāyam adhīyīta trirātrīṃ sāvitrīṃ gāyatrīm anvātirecayati varo dakṣiṇā vareṇaiva varaṃ spṛṇoty ātmā hi vara" iti. prāyaścittasmaraṇāc ca doṣāstīti cet.

[57.19] yathāmṛtārthaṃ yatatāṃ surāṇām abdhimanthane /
[57.20] pārijātādikāny āsan phalāny aprārthitāny api // [NāradaP.]

[57.21] evaṃ mokṣaikacittānāṃ yatatām īśasaṃsmṛtau /
[57.22] bhavanti siddhayo divyāḥ puṇya*{511}* puṇyānubandhi yat //" ityādi [NāradaP]

[57.23] tatraiva: "surātithyarcanakṛte gurubhṛtyartham eva ca /
[57.24] sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyāt na tu duṣyet svayaṃ tataḥ //" [NāradaP]

!{511}! Lies: puṇyaṃ.

[58.1-2] iti ca smaraṇāt. ataḥ śāstroktamārgeṇa bhagavadyajanavidhau pravṛttānāṃ tattatkarmasu dakṣiṇāpratigrahe kṛte 'pi na doṣaḥ.

[ālayārcanāyāḥ mahābhāratādisaṃmatatvam]

[58.3] gṛhārcanāvyatirekeṇālayārcanā bhāratādiṣu pratipāditā dṛśyate. yathā -

[58.4] mahābhārate āśvamedhike "kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo 'sī"ty ādi. [MBh 14 App. 4.1652pr]

[58.5] viṣṇudharmottare ṣaṣṭhe 'dhyāye:
[58.6] "yas tu devagṛhasyārthaṃ prākāraṃ parikalpayet /
[58.7] sa tu svargaṃ samāsadya vimānādhipatir bhavet // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]

[58.8] yas tu devālayasyāgre śilādārubhir eva vā /
[58.9] karoti toraṇaṃ ramyaṃ sa tu svargādhipo bhavet // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]

[58.10] yas tu devālayaṃ viṣṇor dāruśailamṛdā tathā /
[58.11] iṣṭakākalpitaṃ vāpi kuryāt tasya phalaṃ bahu // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]

[58.12] ahanyahany aśvamedha- sahasrāṇi karoti yaḥ /
[58.13] prāpnoti maṇḍapaṃ viṣṇoḥ yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]

[58.14] keśavasya sa tallokam akṣayyaṃ pratipadyate /
[58.15] pratimārthaṃ mahāviṣṇos sādhayed uttamāṃ śilām // [ViṣṇudharmottaraP ]

[58.16] ṣaṣṭirvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate //" iti. [ViṣṇudharmottaraP ]

[58.17-19] eteṣāṃ ca prākāratoraṇamaṇḍapavigrahaśilādīṇāṃ gṛhadevatāsvasaṃbhavaḥ śrīvaikhānasasaṃhitāsu pratipāditaḥ. prasaṅgād arcakamahimādīha kathyate.

[arcakamāhātmyam]

[58.20] bṛhannāradīye: "sa kadācin mahāpāpo jantūnāmantakopamaḥ //" [BṛhannāradaP]

[58.21] ity ārabhya
[58.22] "tasyopavanamadhyasthaṃ ramyaṃ keśavamandiram /
[58.23] chāditaṃ hemakavacaiḥ dṛṣṭvā vyādho mudā yayau // [BṛhannāradaP]

[58.24] harāmy atra suvarṇāni bahūnīti sa niścitaḥ /
[58.25] jagāma viṣṇubhavanaṃ kīnāśaś cauryalolupaḥ // [BṛhannāradaP]

[59.1] tatrāpaśyad dvijavaraṃ śāntaṃ tattvārthakovidam /
[59.2] paricaryāparaṃ viṣṇor udaṅkaṃ tapasāṃ nidhim // [BṛhannāradaP]

[59.3] ekāntinaṃ dayāluñ ca nisspṛhaṃ dhyānalolupam /
[59.4] dṛṣṭvā taṃ lubdhako mene svakāryasyāntarāyinam // [BṛhannāradaP]

[59.5] devasya dravyajātan tu samādātumanā niśi //" [BṛhannāradaP]

[59.6-7] ityādināpṛthagālayārcakasadbhāvādikaṃ uktvā svakāryāntarāya bhūtārcakahiṃsāyāṃ pravṛttasya tasya maraṇam api pratipādya.

[viṣṇupādodakamāhātmyam]

[59.8] "udaṅkaḥ patitaṃ prekṣya lubdhakantu dayāparaḥ /
[59.9] viṣṇupādodakenainam abhyaṣiñ canmahāmuniḥ //

[59.10] haripādodakas parśāl lubdhako vītakalmaṣaḥ /
[59.11] divyaṃ vimānamāruhya munim enam athābravīt //"

[59.12] iti bhagavatpādodakamāhātmyaṃ ca pratipāditam.

[59.13] tatraiva - yajñadhvajavītihotrasaṃvāde:

[ālaye dīpasthāpanādeḥ phalam]

[59.14] "sa kadācit tu kāmāndho rantukāmaḥ parastriyam /
[59.15] śūnyaṃ pūjādibhir viṣṇor mandiraṃ prāptavān niśi //

[59.16] tatra kāmopabhogārthaṃ śayituṃ tena kāminā /
[59.17] svavastraprāntato brahman kṛtaṃ taddeśamārjanam //

[59.18] yāvantaḥ pāṃsukaṇikāḥ tena sammārjitās tadā /
[59.19] tāvaj janmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tadaiva kṣayam āgatam //

[59.20] pradīpaḥ sthāpitas tatra suratārthaṃ dvijottama /
[59.21] tenāpi tasya duṣkarma niśśeṣaṃ kṣayam āgatam //

[59.22] avaśenāpi yatkarma kṛtvemāṃ siddhim āgataḥ /
[59.23] bhaktimadbhiḥ praśāntaiś ca kiṃ punas samyagarcanāt //

[ālayapradakṣiṇaphalam]

[60.1] tasmāc chruṇuta viprendrāḥ devo nārāyaṇo 'vyayaḥ /
[60.2] jñānato 'jñānato vāpi pūjakānāṃ vimuktidaḥ //"

[60.3] tathā tatraiva - indrasudharmasaṃvāde:
[60.4] "ahamāsaṃ purā śakra gṛdhraḥ pāpāvaśeṣataḥ /
[60.5] sthitaś ca bhūmibhāge vai amedhyāmiṣabhojanaḥ //

[60.6] ekadāhaṃ viṣṇugṛhe prākāre saṃsthitaḥ prabhoḥ /
[60.7] patito vyādhaśastreṇa sāyaṃ viṣṇugṛhaṃ gate //

[60.8] mayi kaṇṭhagataprāṇe kaścit śvā māṃsalolupaḥ /
[60.9] jagraha māṃ svavaktreṇa śvabhir anyair abhidrutaḥ //

[60.10] gataḥ pradakṣiṇākāraṃ viṣṇos tanmandiraṃ prabhoḥ /
[60.11] tenaiva tuṣṭim āpannaḥ antarātmā jaganmayaḥ //

[60.12] mama cāpi śunaś cāpi dattavān paramaṃ padam /
[60.13] pradakṣiṇākāratabis hier noch Telugu vergleichenyā gatasya sadṛśaṃ phalam //

[60.14] samprāptaṃ tu mayā śakra*{512}* kiṃ punas samyag arcanāt /
[60.15] ye 'rcayanti sadā bhaktyā nārāyaṇam anāmayam /
[60.16] tān arcayanti vibudhā brahmādyā devatāgaṇāḥ //"*{513}* iti

[amedhyāni pañca]

[60.17] evam āśvamedhike: "loke trīṇy apavitrāṇi pañcāmedhyāni bhārata / [MBh 13, App. 4.3249]

[60.18] śvā ca śūdraś śvapākaś ca tryapavitrāṇi pāṇḍava* /{514}* [MBh 13, App. 4.3250]

[60.19] devalaḥ kukkuṭo yūpaḥ udakyā vṛṣalīpatiḥ //" [MBh 13, App. 4.3251]

[60.20] pañcamedhyāni*{515}* iti.

[bhagavatpūjādyanadhikāriṇaḥ]

!{512}! DHN[T] 253: samprāptaṃ vibudhaśreṣṭha. !{513}! Ähnlich zitiert als "Bṛhannāradīyapurāṇa" in DHN[D] 119.3-4. !{514}! MBh: śvā ca śūdraś śvapākaś cety apavitrāṇi pāṇḍava. !{515}! DHN[T] 253 om. pañcamedhyāni.

[61.1] nārhanti tasmāt kurvīta dvāraṃ yavanikāvṛtam //"

[61.2-3] iti pratipādanāt bhagavadarcanadarśanādiṣu yogyatārahitānāṃ nikṛṣṭānāṃ (devalakānāṃ) autkṛṣṭyaṃ na sambhavati.*{516}*

[advārakabhagavadyājinām utkṛṣṭatvam]

[61.11] jagat pavitrās te nityaṃ viṣṇum abhyarcayanti ye /

[vaikhānasānāṃ bhagavatprītipātratvam]

[61.13-16] vyāsenapi*{524}* ānuśāsanike (90. adhyāye) pātrakathanāvasare*{525}* devalakānām apātratāṃ satkarmaniṣṭhānāṃ pātratāñ ca pratipādya svavacanadṛḍhīkaraṇārthaṃ "vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsan"*{526}* iti bhagavatprītiviṣayāṇāṃ*{527}* vaikhānasānāṃ vacanam api śrūyate iti pratipāditam. yathā:

[61.17] *{528}*"ṛṣīṇāṃ samayaṃ nityaṃ ye rakṣanti yudhiṣṭhira* /{529}*

[61.18] niścitāḥ sarvadharmajñās tān devā brāhmaṇān viduḥ // [MB.h 13.9.42]

[61.19] svādhyāyaniṣṭhā ṛṣayo*{530}* jñānaniṣṭhās tathaiva ca /
[61.20] taponiṣṭhāś ca boddhavyāḥ karmaniṣṭhāś ca bhārata // [MBh 13.9.43]

[61.21] kavyāni jñānaniṣṭhebhyaḥ pratiṣṭhāpyāni bhārata /
[61.22] tatra ye brāhmaṇān ke cin na ca nindanti te varāḥ* //{531}* [MBh 13.9.44]

[61.23] ye tu nindanti jalpeṣu na tāñ śrāddheṣu bhojayet /
[61.24] brāhmaṇā ninditā rājan hanyus tripuruṣaṃ kulam* //{532}* [MBh 13.9.45]

[62.1] vaikhānasānāṃ vacanam ṛṣīṇāṃ śrūyate nṛpa /
[62.2] dūrād eva parīkṣeta brāhmaṇān vedapāragān /
[62.3] priyo vā yadi vā dveṣyaḥ teṣu tac chrāddham āvapet* //{533}* [MBh 13.9.46]

[62.4] yaḥ sahasraṃ sahasrāṇāṃ bhojayed anṛcāṃ naraḥ /
[62.5] ekas tān mantravit pūtaḥ sarvān arhati bhārata* //{534}*" [MBh 13.9.47]

[aṣṭākṣarādimantrajapaniṣṭhānāṃ mahimā]

[62.6-7] evaṃ aṣṭākṣara dvādaśākṣara puruṣasūktādimantrajapaniṣṭhānāṃ darśanena brahmahā 'pi śuddhyatīti purāṇoktam. yathā*{535}*:
[62.8] *{536}*padmapurāṇe: "sāṅgaṃ samantraṃ sanyāsaṃ sarṣicchandodhidaivatam /
[62.9] sadīkṣāvidhi sadhyānaṃ sayantraṃ dvādaśākṣaram // [Padma.P ]

[62.10] sāṣṭākṣarañ ca mantreśaṃ ye japanti narottamāḥ /
[62.11] tān dṛṣṭvā brahmahā śuddhyet kiṃ punar vaiṣṇavas svayam //" iti [PadmaP ]

[62.12-14] śruyate 'pi. "yo ha vai nārāyaṇasyāṣṭākṣaraṃ padam adhyeti anupabravas sarvam āyur eti vindate prājāpatyaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ gaupatyaṃ tato 'mṛtatvam aśnute tato 'mṛtatvam aśnuta iti".

[62.15] śrīpāñcarātre kapiñjalasaṃhitāyām:
[62.16] "yājanādhyāpanayutaḥ śiṣyānugrahakārakaḥ /
[62.17] ācārya iti vijñeyo mantratantraparāyaṇaḥ* //{537}* [KapiñjalaS]

[62.18] āśrame vā vane vā 'pi sa vaikhānasa ucyate* /{538}*

[62.19] grāmyadharmāṇi sarvāṇi varjayed vanavāsakaḥ //"*{539}* iti. [KapiñjalaS]

[62.20] yamasmṛtau: "yo 'nucānaṃ*{540}* dvijaṃ martyo hatavān arthalobhataḥ /
[62.21] sa vadet pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ jalasthaś cintayed dharim* //{541}*"

[62.22-24] iti kevalāṣṭākṣaramantrajapaniṣṭhānām apy evaṃ vidhāḥ prabhāvāḥ śrūyanta iti cet śrutismṛtivihitais tair eva mantraiḥ advārakabhagavadarcane mukhyādikāriṇāṃ vaikhānasānāṃ kaimutikanyāyasiddham autkṛṣṭyaṃ kenāpodituṃ śakyam.*{542}*

!{533}! MBh: priyān vā yadi vā dveṣyāṃs. !{534}! MBh: ekas tān mantravit prītaḥ; DHN[T] 257: ekas tān mantravit putas sarvam arhati bhārateti (10 adhyāye). !{535}! DHN[T] 258: brahmahā śuddhyatītyuktaṃ. !{536}! DHN[T] 258-259 verschiebt das Padmapurāṇa-Zitat weiter nach hinten und liest somit statt DHN[D] 62.8-19: śruyate hi. "yo ha vai nārāyaṇasyāṣṭākṣaraṃ padam adhyeti anapabruvas sarvam āyur eti vindate prājāpatyaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ gaupatyaṃ tato 'mṛtatvam aśnute tato 'mṛtatvam aśnuta iti". aṣṭākṣaraparā vaikhānasāḥ. kapiñjalasaṃhitāyām: yājanādhyāpanayutaḥ śiṣyān ugrahakārakaḥ / ācārya iti vijñeyo mantratantraparāyaṇaḥ // āśram.e vā vane vā 'pi sa vaikhānasa ucyate / grāmyadharmāṇi sarvāṇi varjayed vanavāsaka // iti. padmapurāṇe: sāṅgaṃ samantraṃ sanyāsaṃ sarṣicchandadaivatam / sadīkṣāvidhi sadhyānaṃ sayajñaṃ (yantraṃ?) dvādaśākṣaram // aṣṭākṣarañ ca mantreśaṃ ye japanti narottamāḥ / tān dṛṣṭvā brahmahā śuddhyet kiṃ punar vaiṣṇavas svayam // iti. !{537}! Ebenfalls zitiert als "Kapiñjalasaṃhitā" in DHN[D] 93.4-5. !{538}! Vgl. das Zitat aus "Kapiñjalasaṃhitā" in DHN[D] 93.6-7: āśrame vā vane vā 'pi putradārasamāhitaḥ / aṣṭākṣaraparo nityaṃ sa vaikhānasa ucyate //. !{539}! Ebenfalls zitiert als "Kapiñjalasaṃhitā" in DHN[D] 93.8. !{540}! DHN[T] 260: 'nūcānaṃ. !{541}! DHN[T] 260: cintayan harim. !{542}! DHN[T] 261-263 statt DHN[D] 62.22-24: kevalāṣṭākṣarādimantrajapaniṣṭhānām evaṃvidhāḥ prabhā hiś śrūyante (iti) cet śrutismṛtisūtravihitais tair eva mantraiḥ advārakabhagavadarcane mukhyādikāriṇāṃ kaimutikanyāya siddham utkṛṣṭatvādikaṃ neti. śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇādyarthatattvān abhijñād aprāmāṇikodanākalitapūrvottarān mahāsāhasikodunmattādanyaḥ vā brūyāt? punardevalakatvādivicāraḥ.

[devalakanirūpaṇam]

[63.1-3] kiñca - yathā vaikhānasānām utpattyādikaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaṃ tathā itareṣāṃ viśeṣeṇa pratipāditañ cet tadā vaikhānasasāmyam itareṣāṃ syāt. tathā na dṛśyate hi.

[63.4] atha vastuto devalakā nirūpyante.*{543}*
[63.5] vaikhānase: "avaikhānasavipro yaḥ pūjayed ālaye harim /
[63.6] sa vai devalako nāma havyakavyabahiṣkṛtaḥ* //{544}*

[63.7] vaikhānasakule jātaḥ pāñcarātreṇa dīkṣitaḥ /

[63.8] na dīkṣito na sañjāto (?) lobhān mohān madarcanam* /{545}*

[63.9] kuryāc cet tu viśeṣeṇa bhaved devalakas to saḥ //"*{546}*

[devalakatraividyam]

[63.10] pāñcarātre saṃkarṣaṇasaṃhitāyām: "karmadevalakāḥ kecit kalpadevalakāḥ pare /
[63.11] śuddhadevalakāś cānye tridhā devalakāḥ smṛtāḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

[karmadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[63.12] arthārthī kālanirdeśī yo devaṃ pūjayet sa hi /
[63.13] karmadevalako nāma sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

[63.14] pāñcarātravidhānajño dīkṣāvirahito 'rcakaḥ /
[63.15] caturvedādhikāro 'pi kalpadevalakaḥ smṛtaḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

[63.16] āgamoktavidhānajño bhadrakālyupajīvakaḥ*{547}* /
[63.17] śuddhadevalakaḥ proktaḥ sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

[63.18] ārṣoktena vidhānena devalatvaṃ na vidyate /
[63.19] tasmāt sarvaprayatnena vaidikenaiva pūjayet //" iti [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā]

[63.20] śivaśekharatantre - rudraḥ:
[63.21] "atha devalakān vakṣye śṛṇu devi samāhitā /
[63.22] karmadevalakāḥ kecit kalpadevalakāḥ pare // [Śivaśekharatantra]

[63.23] śuddhadevalakās tv anye tridhā devalakāsmṛtāḥ /
[63.24] anyasūtroktamārgeṇa yas saṃvatsarapūjakaḥ //

!{543}! DHN[T] 263-4 statt DHN[D] 63.1-4: punar devalakatvādivicāraḥ. kiñca - yathā vaikhānasānām utpattyādikaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaṃ evam itareṣāṃ brāhmaṇasāmānyatvena vinā viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaṃ cet tadānīmetādṛguṇaviśiṣṭā vayam iti. tair vaktum ucitam anyathā asaṃtaṃ? nindyām ātmastutiṃ mūḍhetarāḥ svaparagataviśeṣajñāḥ ke vā brūyaḥ? devalakalakṣaṇaṃ nirūpyate yathā. !{544}! Dieser Vers ist ähnlich als "Purātantra" zitiert in DHN[D] 38.12-13. !{545}! DHN[T] 273: madarjanam. !{546}! Vgl. ĀS 19.15: vaikhānasakule jātaḥ pañcarātreṇa dīkṣitaḥ / na dīkṣito na jāto vai sa vai devalakas smṛtaḥ. !{547}! DHN[T] 274: rudrkāḷyupajīvakaḥ.

[Śivaśekharatantra]

[kalpadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[64.1] adīkṣitaḥ svayaṃ tantre karmadevalakas tu saḥ /
[64.2] anenaiva prakāreṇa vatsaratryapūjakaḥ /
[64.3] kalpadevalakaḥ proktaḥ sa vai śailasute dhruvam // [Śivaśekharatantra]

[śuddhadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[64.4] ananujñātam ācāryāt āgamaṃ śuśruve ca yaḥ /
[64.5] śīlataḥ tasya śiṣyaś ca śuddhadevalakāv ubhau // [Śivaśekharatantra]

[trividhasyāpi devalakatvasya rudrādiviṣayakatā]

[64.6] tridhā devalakatvaṃ tu na viṣṇuviṣaye kvacit /
[64.7] rudrakālyādiviṣayam etad āgamasaṃmatam //" iti [Śivaśekharatantra]

[64.8] smṛtyantare: "śarvaṃ sūryaṃ tathā candraṃ durgādī rudradevatāḥ /
[64.9] yo 'rcayet paṇapūrvaṃ saḥ sadyaḥ patati mānavaḥ //

[64.10] durgā ca bhadrakālī ca buddhaś ca kṣetrapālakaḥ /
[64.11] pañcapūjā ca ity ete pañcadevalakāḥ smṛtāḥ //

[64.12] ādityam ambikāṃ viṣṇuṃ gaṇanāthaṃ maheśvaram /
[64.13] gṛhe pūjā ca ity ete pañcadevalakāḥ smṛtāḥ (?) //" iti*{548}*

[64.14] *{549}*viṣṇudharmottare: "caṇḍikāyāś ca durgāyā jyeṣṭāyā bhairavasya ca /
[64.15] rudrasya pūjakā ye vai te vai devalakāḥ smṛtāḥ //" iti [ViṣṇudharmottaraP ]

[64.16] viṣṇu: "devārcanaparo yo 'pi*{550}* parārthaṃ vittakāṅkṣayā /
[64.17] caturvedadharo vipraḥ sa caṇḍālasamo bhaved* //{551}*" iti [ViṣṇuP ]

[64.18-19] *{552}*evam ebhir vacanaiḥ śāstrānanumatamārgeṇa pūjakānāṃ devatāntarapūjakānām eva ca devalakatvaṃ siddhyatīti sphuṭam avagamyate.
[64.20] kiñca: "vṛṣo dharmas samākhyataḥ tasya yaḥ kurute layam /
[64.21] vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devā nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api //"

!{548}! DHN[T] 275 ins. iti kiñca hārīta: vaikhānasās ti ye viprā haripūjanatatparāḥ. na te devalakā proktā viṣṇupādābjasaṃśrayāḥ iti. smṛtiratnākare atri: vaidikenaiva vidhinā daṃbhalobhavivarjitaḥ pūjayed bhaktito viṣṇuṃ sa hi devalako na vai iti. Zitiert als "Hārīta" in DHN[D] 65.3-4 und als "Smṛtyarthasāra" in DHN[D] 65.5-6. !{549}! DHN[T] zieht hier das Zitat von Hārīta aus DHN[D] 65.3-4 und aus Smṛtyarthasāra aus DHN[D] 65.5-6 vor: hārīta: vaikhānasās ti ye viprā haripūjanatatparāḥ /na te devalakā proktā viṣṇupādābjasaṃśrayāḥ // iti. smṛtiratnākare atri: vaidikenaiva vidhinā daṃbhalobhavivarjitaḥ pūjayed bhaktito viṣṇuṃ sa hi devalako na vai iti. !{550}! DHN[T] 276: devārcanaparo hy āsīt. !{551}! DHN[T] 276: sa caṇḍālīsamo bhaśet. !{552}! DHN[T] 276 statt DHN[D] 64.18-65.7: kiñca devaśabdasya dhātvarthe vicāryamāṇe "div" krīḍāvijigīṣāvyavahāradyutistutimodamadasvapnakāntigatiṣv" iti devaṃ vedaśāstroktamārgaṃ liyata iti devalakaḥ svārthe "ka" pratyayaḥ. "vṛṣo dharmas samākhyataḥ tasya yaḥ kurute layam / vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devā nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api //" iti vṛṣalaśabdavyutpattir darśitā.

[devalakaśabdanirvacanam]

[64.22-65.2] iti vṛṣalaśabdo yathā vedaśāstroktamārgalayakārake vyutpāditaḥ, tathā devalakśabdo 'pi "div krīḍāvijigīṣāvyavahāradyutistutimodamadasvapnakāntigatiṣv" iti dhātvarthānusāreṇa gatyaparaparyāyamārgārthakadivdhātughaṭitassan vedoktamārgalayaprāpake vyutpādayituṃ śakyate iti tatpratīpeṣu vedamārgapratiṣṭhāpakeṣu vaikhānaseṣu na sarvātmanā pravartate. tathā ca:
[65.3] hārītaḥ: "vaikhānasās tu ye viprā haripūjanatatparāḥ /
[65.4] na te devalakāḥ proktā viṣṇupādābjasaṃśrayāt* //{553}*" iti [Vṛddhahārīta 8.78]

[vaikhānasānaṃ devalakaśabdavācyatvābhāvaḥ]

[65.5] smṛtyarthasāre: atri: "vaidikenaiva vidhinā dambhalobhavivarjitaḥ /
[65.6] pūjayed bhaktito viṣṇuṃ sa hi devalako na vai* //{554}*" iti

[65.7-8] *{555}*anyathā śrutyuktamārgeṇālayārcakānām api devalakatve tādṛśālayārcanapratipādakānāṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādivacanānāṃ vyarthatā syāt.

[65.9-10] *{556}*nanu - ajñānataḥ kṛtam api bhagavadārādhanam apavargapradañ cet. vinā śāstraṃ anadhikāriṇāpi kṛtaṃ tatapavargapradaṃ kiṃ na syād iti cet. na. bhagavadājñābhaṅgāpatteḥ.
[65.11] yathoktaṃ bhagavatā: "yaś śāstravidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥ /
[65.12] na sa siddhim avāpnoti na sukhaṃ na parāṃ gatim //" iti [MBh 6.38.23]

[65.13] "śrutismṛtī mamaivājñā yas tām ullaṅghya vartate /
[65.14] ājñācchedī mama drohī madbhakto 'pi na vaiṣṇavaḥ* //{557}*" iti

[65.15] "mama cāpi priyaṃ viṣṇor devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ /
[65.16] mānuṣo vaidikācāraṃ manasā 'pi na laṅghayet //" iti

[65.17-18] *{558}*ataḥ anadhikāriṇā kṛtaṃ śāstrāsammatam iti tantroktaprakāreṇa kṛtam api tat nāpavargapradam.*{559}*
[65.19] nanu: "brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaiḥ /
[65.20] arcanīyaś ca sevyaś ca pūjanīyaś ca mādhavaḥ /
[65.21] sāttvataṃ vidhim āsthāya gītaḥ saṅgarṣaṇena*{560}* yaḥ //"

[tantrānusāripūjāyāḥ apavargapradatvābhāvaḥ]

[65.22-24] *{561}*iti śūdrādīnām api pāñcarātroktamārgeṇārcane adhikāre siddhe kathaṃ tāntrikoktaprakāreṇārcanaṃ kurvataḥ brāhmaṇādeḥ (anadhikāriṇaḥ) tat apavargapradaṃ na bhavatīty ucyata iti ced ucyate.

!{553}! Vṛddhahārīta: na te devalakāḥ jñeyā haripādābjasaṃśrayāt. !{554}! Nach Kane, HD 2.1: Atri in "Smṛtyarthasāra". Vgl. Kane, HD 2.1, und HD 1.2, S. 1156. !{555}! DHN[T] 277 statt DHN[D] 65.7-8: anyathā śrutismṛtipurāṇapañcarātrādiṣu pratipāditānāṃ vacanānāṃ vyarthatā syāt. śarvādyarcanāvidhipratipādakasya bodhāyanasyāpi patitatvaṃ saṃbhavati, tatsūtropajīviṣu tacchiṣyeṣv āpastambādiṣv atyantapātityaṃ kaimutikanyāyasiddhaṃ. !{556}! DHN[T] 277 statt DHN[D] 65.9-10: nanu - ajñānataḥ kṛtam bhagavadārādhanam apavargapradañ ced. anadhikāriṇaś śāstroktamārgeṇa vinā 'py apavargapradaṃ kiṃ na syād iti cen naivaṃ bhagavadājñābhaṅgakṛttvāt. !{557}! Dieser Vers ist auch zitiert in DHN[D] 56.6-7. !{558}! DHN[T] 278 statt DHN[D] 65.17-18: ato 'nadhikāriṇas tāntrikoktaprakāreṇa kurvato 'pavargapradatvaṃ? na saṃbhavati. !{559}! In DHN[D] 69.1-2 wird auf diese Aussage Bezug genommen. !{560}! Lies mit DHN[T] 278: saṅkarṣaṇena. !{561}! DHN[T] 278 statt DHN[D] 65.22-24: iti śūdrādīnām api pāñcarātre 'dhikāro vidhīyate kathaṃ vā tāntrikoktena prakāreṇa kurvato 'pavargapradaṃ na bhavatīty ucyata iti ced ucyate.

[caturvidhatantreṣu ekatra dīkṣitasya tantrāntare 'nadhikāraḥ]

[66.1] "prathamaṃ mantrasiddhāntaṃ dvitīyañ cāgamāhvayam / [PādmaS caryāpāda 19.112cd]

[66.2] tṛtīyaṃ tantrasiddhāntaṃ tantrāntaramataḥ param* //{562}*" [PādmaS caryāpāda 19.113ab]

[66.3] iti caturvidheṣu siddhānteṣu

[66.4] "ekatra dīkṣitas tantre siddhānte vā dvijottama* /{563}*

[66.5] kriyāṃ na kuryād anyatra karṣaṇādi caturmukha // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 19.131]

[66.6] ācāryakam athārtvijyaṃ pūjāñ ca madhuvidviṣaḥ /
[66.7] mantre deve ca siddhānte tad evāsya hi yujyate* //{564}*" [PādmaS caryāpāda 19.132]

[66.8] iti caturvidhatantreṣu ekatra dīkṣitasya tantrāntare praveśayogyatābhāvasya pratipādanāt*{565}*.

[66.9] "ekagotrasamutpannaṃ pañcagotraṃ pṛthak pṛthak / ity ārabhya

[66.10] sūtraṃ kātyāyanaṃ śākhāṃ yājuṣaṃ*{566}* śuklam eva ca //

[66.11] aupagāyanaśāṇḍilyau bhāradvājo 'tha gautamaḥ /
[66.12] mauñjāyanis tu pañcaite pāñcarātrādhikāriṇaḥ* //{567}*"

[66.13] ity adhikāribhedasya vidhīyamānatvāt.

[āpastambādisūtrasaṃskṛtasya pāñcarātroktasaṃskārayogyatābhāvaḥ]

[66.14] "caturṇām api varṇānām itareṣāñ ca tadbhuvām /
[66.15] dīkṣā samaiva sarveṣām ācāras tantravartmanā //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 21.55]

[tantroktaprakāreṇa dīkṣitānām eva tantroktārcanāyām adhikāraḥ]

[66.16-18] ityāpastambādisūtraiḥ*{568}* saṃskṛtasya pāñcarātroktamārgeṇa niṣekādisaṃskārayogyatābhavakathanāt.*{569}* tāntrikoktaprakāreṇa dīkṣitānām eva tantroktārcanāyām adhikāritva sambhavāt.

[paradharmānuṣṭhātuḥ patitatvādi]

[66.19] "svasūtre vartamāne tu parasūtreṇa vartate /
[66.20] apramāṇam ṛṣiṃ kṛtvā so 'ndhe tamasi majjati //"

[66.21] "svakīyadharmam utsṛjya paradharmaṃ ya āśrayet* /{570}*

[66.22] patitas sa bhaved āśu sadya eva na saṃśayaḥ //"

[66.23] "svasūtrasya parityāgāt parasūtrasamāśrayāt /
[66.24] sadyaḥ patati vai vipro na vedasya samāśraye //"*{571}*

!{562}! PādmaS: turyaṃ tantrāntaraṃ bhavet. !{563}! PādmaS: dvijottamaḥ. !{564}! DHN[T] 278: tad evāpi na yujyata. PādmaS: ācāryatvam athārtvijyaṃ pūjāyāṃ madhuvidviṣaḥ / tantrabhede ca siddhāntabhede cāpi na yujyate //; v.l.: tantrabhede ca siddhānte tad evāpi na yujyate. !{565}! DHN[T] 278: praveśayogyatābhāt. !{566}! DHN[T] 279: śākhā yajuṣāṃ. !{567}! Vgl. ĪśvaraS 21.519: pañcāyudhāṃśāste pañca śāṇḍilyaś caupagāyanaḥ / mauñjyāyanaḥ kauśikaś ca bhāradvājaś ca yoginaḥ //. !{568}! DHN[T] 279: āpastambādisūtreṣu. !{569}! DHN[T] 279: niṣekādisaṃskārayogyatābhāvāt. !{570}! DHN[T] 280: samāśrayet. !{571}! Dieser Vers ist ähnlich zitiert in DHN[D] 35.4-5.

[67.1] "śākhāṃ śikhāṃ tathā puṇḍraṃ samayācāram eva ca /
[67.2] pūrvair ācaritaṃ kuryād anyathā patito bhavet //"

[67.3] "yas svaśākhāṃ parityajya paraśākhāsu vartate /
[67.4] śākhāraṇḍas sa vijñeyas sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ* //{572}*" [ĀS 4.59]

[67.5] "yas svadharmaṃ parityajya paradharmaṃ niṣevate /
[67.6] pāṣaṇḍinaṃ tam āhur vai nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api //" iti.

[67.7] bhagavān: "śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt /
[67.8] svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ* //{573}*" iti. [MBh 6.25.35]

[67.9] vyāsa: "svadharmaṃ yas samutsṛjya paradharmaṃ samāśrayet /
[67.10] anāpadi sa vidvadbhiḥ patitaḥ parikīrtitaḥ //"

[67.11-12] *{574}*ityādibhiś ca vacanaiḥ paradharmānuṣṭhātuḥ patitatvādismaraṇāc ca anyasūtroktaprakāreṇa tāntrikoktena mārgeṇa vā bāhmaṇādibhir*{575}* api anadhikāribhiḥ bhagavadārādhanaṃ kartuṃ na śakyate.

[śūdrasya pūjāyām anadhikāraḥ]

[67.13] tarhi "brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ" ityādi *{576}*bhāratavacanasya kā gatir iti cet - ucyate.

[67.14] *{577}*mādhavāḥ: mukhyatvena advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāritvena nirūpitaiḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjanīyaḥ.

[67.15-16] *{578}*itaraiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiś cārcanīyaḥ. śūdraiḥ strībhiś ca yathārham ijyas sevyaś ca iti tasya vacanasyārthaḥ.
[67.17] "... śūdraiḥ strībhis tathetaraiḥ /
[67.18] yathārham ijyas sevyaś ca nityaṃ sarveśvaro hariḥ //"

[67.19-22] iti bhāradvājavacanāt "arghyāntam arcanaṃ proktaṃ havirantañ ca pūjanam //" ity arcanapūjanayoḥ bhinnārthakatvapratipādanāt, sarvair ekarītyā pūjane 'bhimate ekapadasyaiva paryāptatvāt itarayoḥ padayor vaiyarthyāpātāc ca. anyathā śūdrasyāpi pūjārcanādiṣv adhikārāṅgīkāre śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇādivirodho bhavet.

[67.23-25] śūdrasyānadhikārapratipādakāni vacanāni caitāni. śruti "tasmāc chūdro yajñe 'navakḷptaḥ. sa hi devatā anvasṛjata tasmāc chūdro bahupaśur ayajñīyo daiva" iti.

!{572}! ĀS: svaśākhāṃ samparityajya paraśākhānusārataḥ / śākhāraṇḍas sa vijñeyas sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ //. !{573}! Dieser Vers ist auch in DHN[D] 47.10-11 zitiert. !{574}! DHN[T] 280 statt DHN[D] 67.11-12: iti paradharmānuṣṭhātuḥ patitatvādisambhavāc ca anyasūtroktamārgeṇa vā tāntrikoktena mārgeṇa vā bhagavadārādhanaṃ kartuṃ na śakyate. !{575}! Lies mit DHN[T] 280: brāhmaṇādibhir. !{576}! DHN[T] 281 om. tarhi "brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ" ityādi. !{577}! DHN[T] 281 statt DHN[D] 67.14: mukhyatvenādvārakabhagavadyajanādhikāritvena nirūpitaiḥ pūjanīyaḥ. !{578}! DHN[T] 281 statt DHN[D] 67.15-25: itaraiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiś cārcanīyaḥ. śūdraiḥ strībhirathetaraiḥ yathārham ijyas sevyaś ca nityam sarveśvaro harir" iti anyathā. śrutismṛtiḥ sūtrapurāṇādīnāṃ virodhaḥ. "arghyāntam arcanaṃ proktaṃ havirantañ ca pūjanam /" ity vacanād ekatarapadavaiyarthyaṃ. śūdrasyārcanādāv anadhikāraḥ kā vā śrutir iti cet "tasmāc chūdro yajñe nānaklīptaḥ. sa hi devatā anvasṛjata tasmāc chūdro bahupaśur ayajñīyā daivaḥ iti.

[68.1] smṛti: "japas tapas tīrthasevā pravrajyā mantrasādhanam /
[68.2] devatārādhanañ caiva strīśūdrapatitāni ṣaṭ //" iti

[śūdrasyadvijaśuśrūṣaiva dharmaḥ]

[68.3] śrībhāgavate:*{579}* "śuśrūṣaṇaṃ dvijagavāṃ devānāñ cāpy amāyayā /
[68.4] tatra labdhena santoṣaḥ śūdraprakṛtayas tv imāḥ* //{580}*" iti [BhāgavataP 11.17.19]

[68.5] manau: "brāhmaṇasya tapo jñānaṃ tapaḥ kṣatrasya rakṣaṇam /
[68.6] vaiśyasya tu tapo vārtā tapaś śūdrasya sevanam //" iti [ManuDhŚ 11.235]

[68.7] anyatra*{581}*: "yadi śūdras tapaḥ kuryād vedadṛṣṭena vartmanā /
[68.8] iha cāsya parikleśaḥ pretya cāsyāśubhā gatiḥ //" iti.

[68.9-11] kimarthaṃ śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā sarvadā abhihiteti cet - ucyate. janmāntarīyakarmavaśāt jananakāle 'pi tamoguṇair abhibhūtasya tasya śūdrasya tamonirasanārthaṃ dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇā prayuktam.*{582}*

[68.12] āśvamedhike: "udite savitar yasya kriyāyuktasya dhīmataḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1690]

[68.13] caturvedadharasyāpi dehe ṣaḍvṛṣalāḥ sthitāḥ* //{583}* [MBh 14, App. 4.1691]

[68.14] kṣatriye sapta vijñeyā vaiśye tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ* /{584}* [MBh 14, App. 4.1692]

[68.15] niyatāḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha śūdre 'ṣṭāviṃśatiḥ khalu* //{585}*" ity ārabhya [MBh 14, App. 4.1693]

[68.16] "rāgadveṣau ca mohaś ca pāruṣyañ ca nṛśaṃsatā* /{586}* [MBh 14, App. 4.3340]

[68.17] śāṭhyañ ca dīrghavairañ ca atimānamanārjavam* //{587}* [MBh 14, App. 4.3341]

[68.18] anṛtañ cāpavādaś ca paiśunyam atilobhatā* /{588}* [MBh 14, App. 4.3342]

[68.19] hiṃsā steyaṃ mṛṣāvādo vañcanā roṣalobhate* //{589}* [MBh 14, App. 4.3343]

[68.20] abuddhatā ca nāstikyaṃ bhayam ālasyam eva ca* /{590}* [MBh 14, App. 4.3344]

[68.21] aśaucañ cākṛtajñatvaṃ dambhatā stambha eva ca* //{591}* [MBh 14, App. 4.3345]

[68.22] niṣkṛteś cāpy avijñānaṃ janane śūdram āviśan* /{592}* [MBh 14, App. 4.3346]

[68.23] dṛṣṭvā pitāmahaḥ śūdram abhibhūtan tu tāmasaiḥ // [MBh 14, App. 4.3347]

[68.24] dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ śūdrāṇān tu prayuktavān / [MBh 14, App. 4.3348]

[68.25] naśyanti tāmasā bhāvāḥ śūdrasya dvijabhaktitaḥ //" iti. [MBh 14, App. 4.3349]

!{579}! DHN[T] 282: śūdrasya śuśrūśa: bhāgavate. !{580}! BhāgavataP: śuśrūṣaṇaṃ dvijagavāṃ devānāṃ cāpy amāyayā / tatra labdhena santoṣaḥ śūdraprakṛtayas tv imāḥ. !{581}! DHN[T] 282: ṛtaṃ tapa ityādi. !{582}! DHN[T] 283 statt DHN[D] 68.6-11: śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣāvidhāne hetuḥ. kimarthaṃ śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā sarvadā abhihiteti cet - janmāntarakarmavaśāt jananakāle 'pi tamoguṇair abhibhūtasya tamoguṇanirasanārthaṃ dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇo prayuktam. !{583}! MBh: caturvedavidaś cāpi dehe ṣaḍvṛṣalāḥ smṛtāḥ. !{584}! DHN[T] 283 mit MBh: kṣatriyāḥ sapta vijñeyā vaiśyās tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ. !{585}! DHN[T] 283 mit MBh: niyatāḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha śūdrāṇām ekaviṃśatiḥ. !{586}! MBh: rāgo dveṣaś ca mohaś ca. !{587}! MBh: śāṭhyañ ca dīrghavairitvam; DHN[T] 283: śārthañ. !{588}! DHN[T] 294: anṛtañ cāpavādaṃ ca . !{589}! MBh: roṣalobhata; DHN[T] 284: roṣalobhatā. !{590}! MBh: abuddhitā. !{591}! MBh: ḍambhatā. !{592}! MBh: nikṛtiś cāpi avijñānam jātake śūdram āviśet; DHN[T] 284: aviśat;

[vaikhānasetarasūtriṇāṃ bhagavadārādhanaprakāraḥ]

[69.1] ataḥ tamoguṇābhibhūtasya śūdrasya bhagavadyajanādhikāro nāsty eva.*{593}*

[69.2-7] nanv eṣāṃ*{594}* śaunakādyuktaprakāreṇa bhagavadārādhane 'dhikāro bhaved iti cet*{595}* - tad asat. tatra adhikāriviśeṣapratipādanābhavāt; sāmānyenoktatve 'pi śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇamahābhāratavaikhānasapāñcarātraśaivaśilpajyautiṣādiṣu adhikāriṇāṃ viśiṣya pratipāditatvāt*{596}* sarvaśākhāpratyayanyāyena sāmānyaviśeṣanyāyena "matprakaraṇādhītaṃ sarvaṃ madartham" iti nyāyena prakaraṇasāmyena*{597}*, upāsya devataikyāt guṇopasaṃhāranyāyena ca śaunakādibhir uktārcanāvidher api atraiva paryavasānaṃ yuktam.

[69.8-9] *{598}* itarasūtriṇām katham iti cet - svāśramadharmācaraṇenaiva bhagavadārādhanaphalam siddhyati. yathocyate:
[69.10] smṛtiṣu: "bahvalpaṃ vā svagṛhyoktaṃ yasya karma pracoditam /
[69.11] tasya tāvati śāstrārthe kṛte sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet //" iti

[69.12] śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "varṇāśramācāravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān /
[69.13] viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyas tattoṣakārakaḥ //" [ViṣṇuP 2.8.9]

[69.14] tathānyatra: "varṇāśrameṣu ye dharmāḥ śāstroktā munisattama /
[69.15] teṣu tiṣṭhan naro viṣṇum ārādhayati nānyathā* //{599}* [ViṣṇuP 3.8.19.1-2?]

[69.16] ye yajanti pitṝn devān brāhmaṇāṃś ca hutāśanam /
[69.17] sarvabhūtāntarātmānaṃ viṣṇum eva yajanti te //" iti

[69.18] purāṇāntare: "agnikāryaṃ japaṃ snānaṃ tapas svādhyāyam eva ca /
[69.19] tam evoddiśya deveśaṃ kuru nityam atandritaḥ //

[69.20] prātar utthāya vidhivat snātvā nityaṃ samāhitaḥ /
[69.21] yajet karmabhis tais taiḥ viṣṇuṃ devādisaṃjñitam //"

!{593}! DHN[T] 285: nāsyaiva !{594}! DHN[T] 285 om. nanv eṣāṃ. !{595}! DHN[T] 285: bhagavadārādhanādhikāro 'stīti; vgl. DHN[D] 65.17-18. !{596}! DHN[T] 285: sāmānyatvenoktatvāt śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇabhāratavaikhānasapañcarātraśilpajyautiṣaśaivādiṣu śiṣyapratipāditatvāt. !{597}! DHN[T] 285: prakaraṇasāmyāt. !{598}! Anm. des Herausgebers: māstu śūdrāṇām adhikāraḥ, vaikhānasetarabrāhmaṇānāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ vaiśyānāṃ ca kena mārgeṇa bhagavadārādhanam iti pṛcchati itarasūtriṇām ityādinā. praśnasyāsya pūrvam eva samādhānam uktam. adhunā prakārāntareṇa samādhānam āha - svāśrametyādinā. !{599}! Vgl. DHN[D] 69.14-15.

[70.1] śāṇḍilya:"prakṛttaiś ca nivṛttaiś ca svargadair mokṣadair api /
[70.2] ārādhyo bhagavān eva vedadharmais sanātanaiḥ // [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti.]

[70.3] sa eva sarvathopāsyo nānyas saṃsāratārakaḥ /
[70.4] ubhābhyāṃ jñānakarmabhyām ārādhyo bhagavān hariḥ //" iti [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti]

[70.5] śāntiparvaṇi: "svayambhūvihito*{600}* dharmo yo yasya hi*{601}* nareśvara / [MBh 14, App. 4.222]

[70.6] sa tena kṣapayet pāpaṃ samyag ācaritena hi //" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.223]

[70.7] pādme: "dharmān nijāṃś ca śāstroktān varṇadharmān aśeṣataḥ /
[70.8] pālayantīha ye vaiśyā na te yānti yamālayam //" iti [PadmaP ]

[70.9] smṛtyantare: "śrutismṛtisadācāravihitaṃ karma yas sadā /
[70.10] svasvadharmaṃ prayatnena śreyo 'rthīha samāśrayet //"

[70.11-12] "nānyaḥ panthā vidyate 'yanāye" 'ti "brāhmaṇā vividaśanti yajñena dānena tapasānāśakena" iti ca śrutir imam arthaṃ draḍhayanti.

[70.13-15] ataḥ advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāribhiḥ śrīmadvaikhānasasūtribhis sāmyaṃ keṣāñcid api nopapadyate iti kṛtaṃ pallavitena. etāvatā "akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvāt" iti prathamo hetuḥ nirūpitaḥ.

[70.16] iti prathamahetunirūpaṇam

!{600}! MBh: svayaṃbhuvihito. !{601}! MBh: yo yasyeha.

[71.1] atha dvitīyahetunirūpaṇam

[71.2] athāsya vaikhānasasūtrasya sarvasūtrāṇām āditvaṃ nirūpyate. tathā hi:

[vaikhānasasūtrasya sarvasūtrāpekṣayā āditvam]

[71.3] brahmakaivarte: " yathā munīnāṃ vikhanā ādibhūta udāhṛtaḥ /
[71.4] sūtrāṇāṃ tatpraṇītan tu tathā śreṣṭatamaṃ smṛtam //"*{602}* iti [BrahmakaivartaP ]

[71.5] purātantre bhṛgu: "vedānāṃ vyāsanād arvāk prāgrūpaṃ militan tu yat /
[71.6] tān tu vaikhānasīṃ śākhām iti vedavido viduḥ //"*{603}* ity ārabhya [Purātantra]

[71.7] "vaiṣṇavaṃ sūtram etad dhi sarvasiddhikaraṃ param /
[71.8] ādyatvāt sarvasūtrāṇāṃ vaiṣṇavatvāc ca tat tu vai // [Purātantra]

[71.9] mayānuvartitaṃ tadvat kāśyapātrimarīcibhiḥ //"*{604}* iti [Purātantra]

[71.10] skānde ca: "vaikhānasīṃ mahāśākhāṃ svasūtre viniyuktavān /
[71.11] padmabhūḥ paramo dhātā tasminn ārādhanatrayam* //{605}*

[71.12] uktavān nigamārthānām ācāraṃ pravibhāgaśaḥ*{606}* //" iti [SkandaP ]

[ādau caturaśrasya ravimaṇḍalasya kālāntare vartulatvam]

[71.13-14] sūtrārthaparyālocanayāpi sarvasūtrāditvam asyāvagamyate. yathā -"mukhyād indraś cāgniś ce" ti bhagavanmukhād agnisṛṣṭiḥ śrūyate. tathā:

[71.15] āśvamedhike - bhagavadvacanam:

[71.16] "prathamaṃ manmukhāt sṛṣṭo lokārthe pacanaḥ prabhuḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.2572]

[71.17] sṛṣṭamātro jagatsarvam attum aicchat purā khalu* //{607}* [MBh 14, App. 4.2573]

[71.18] tataḥ praśamitas so 'yam upāsīno mayā purā* /{608}* [MBh 14, App. 4.2574]

[71.19] satatopāsanāt so 'yam aupāsana iti smṛtaḥ //" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.2575]

[71.20-21] evaṃ paramapuruṣamukhāj jātasyaupāsanāgneḥ kuṇḍavidhānādikam atraiva sūtre pratipāditam.

[71.22-24] kiñ ca navagrahamakhe savitṛmaṇḍalasya caturaśratvam ucyate "caturaśraṃ vṛttam ityādinā (sūtre). ādau caturaśrasya sato ravimaṇḍalasya kālāntare vṛttatvakalpanaṃ pramāṇair avagamyate. yathā:

!{602}! Dieser Vers ist auch zitiert als "Brahmakaivartapurāṇa" in DHN[D] 42.9-10. !{603}! Dieser Vers ist als "Purātantra" ähnlich zitiert in DHN[D] 33.21-22. !{604}! Diese drei Halbverse sind auch zitiert als "Purātantra" in DHN[D] 35.20-22. !{605}! Dieser Vers ist ähnlich als "Purātantra" zitiert in 34.9-10. !{606}! Diese drei Halbverse sind als "Skandapurāṇa" auch zitiert in DHN[D] 39.25-40.2. !{607}! MBh: uttamaicchat purā khalu. !{608}! MBh: tataḥ praśamitaḥ so 'gnir upāsyaiva mayā purā.

[72.1] viṣṇupurāṇe: "tejasaś śamanañ cāsya viśvakarmā cakāra ha /
[72.2] bhramimāropya sūryan tu tasya tejo 'vaśātanam // [Viṣṇu.P ]

[72.3] kṛtavān aṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ sa vyaśātayad avyayam /
[72.4] yatsūryād vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaś śātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā // [Viṣṇu.P ]

[72.5] jājjvalyamānam apatat tadbhūmau munisattama //"iti [ViṣṇuP ]

[72.6] evaṃ ca sūryasāvarṇikamanvantaramārabhya ravimaṇḍalasya vṛttākārapratītiḥ.

[72.7-8] tad anusāreṇa bodhāyanādibhiḥ vṛttākāratvaṃ ravimamaṇḍalasyoktam. tataḥ pūrvaṃ caturaśratvam va. tad evāsmin sūtre pratipāditam.

[72.9-10] evaṃ "vānaprastho vaikhānaśāstrasamudācāro vaikhānasa"*{609}* iti vaikhānasasūtram anusmṛtya tṛtīyāśramadharmān bodhāyanaḥ pratipādayati. [BaudhDhS 2.6.11.14]

[72.11-17] tathā āgnivaiśyasūtre "athātas sūtragaṇanāṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. bodhāyanam āpastambaṃ satyāṣāṭhaṃ drāhyāyaṇam āgastyaṃ śākalyam āśvalāyanaṃ śāmbhavīyaṃ kātyāyanam iti navāni pūrvasūtrāṇi. vaikhānasaṃ śaunakīyaṃ bhāradvājam āgnivaiśyaṃ jaiminīyaṃ *{610}* vādhūlaṃ mādhyandinaṃ hiraṇyakeśīyaṃ kauṣītakam iti navāny aparasūtrāṇi. evam aṣṭādaśasūtrāṇy aṣṭādaśasūtrakārāś ca. etāni caturvedamūlāni. pūrvasūtrāṇi śārīrāṇi sāmānyāni bhavanti. uttarasūtrāṇi vaikhānasādīni viṣṇusaṃbandhīni daivikānī" ti vaikhānasasūtrasyāditvaṃ vaiṣṇavatvañ cocyate.

[72.18-19] asya sūtrasyādhikyaṃ ca "ye vaikhānasasūtreṇa saṃskṛtās dvijātaya"*{611}* ityādinā pūrvam eva pratipāditam.

[72.20-21] ataḥ sarvasūtrāṇām ādir idaṃ sūtram iti siddham. tataḥ sarvasūtrottamatvañ cāsyopapadyate iti nirūpito dvitīyo hetuḥ.

[72.22] iti dvitīyahetunitūpaṇam.

!{609}! BaudhDhS: vānaprastho vaikhānasaśāstrasamudācāraḥ. !{610}! Anm. des Herausgebers: atra vādhūlasthāne mādhuryam iti hiraṇyakeśīyasthāne kauṇḍinyam iti ca pāṭhāntaram upalabhyate. !{611}! Dieser Halbvers ist als "Purātantra" zitiert in DHN[D] 36.10.

[tṛtīyahetunirūpaṇam]

[vaikhānasasūtrasya śrutimārgānusāritvam]

[73.1-3] athāsya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya sūtrāntarāpekṣayā vailakṣaṇyāpādakaṃ pratyakṣaśrutimūlakatvam astīti jñāpayituṃ "sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritvād" iti tṛtīyo hetur nirūpyate. tathā hi:

[śuddhācamanavidheḥ śrautatvam]

[73.4-9] śuddhācamanavidhau "yattrir ācāmati tena ṛcaḥ prīṇāti" ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa sūtre "ṛgvedaḥ prīṇātv" ityādinā śuddhācamanam uktam. nanu bodhāyanenāpi śuddhācamanavidhir ukta iti cet satyam. "ācamanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ" ity ārabhya "gokarṇabaddhahastena trir ācamet, prathamaṃ yat pibati tena ṛgvedaṃ prīṇāti yad dvitīyaṃ tena yajurvedaṃ yat tṛtīyaṃ tena sāmavedaṃ prīṇātī"ty ācamanena ṛgvedādīnāṃ prītir bhavatīty uktam. na tu mantraḥ.

[73.10-11] śrutismṛtisūtravihitasya sandhyopāsanasya pradhānabhūtam arghyapradānādikam atraiva pratipāditam. "prātas sūryaś cetyādinācamya āpo hiṣṭhādibhis tisṛbhiḥ prokṣya

[73.12] gāyatryā 'po 'bhimantrya ādityābhimukhaṃ vikṣipya pradakṣiṇaṃ karoti" ityādi.

[73.13-17] bodhāyanenāpi sandhyāvandanavidhir uktaḥ iti cet naivam. "athātas sandhyopāsanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. tīraṃ gatvāprayato 'bhiṣiktaḥ prayato vā nābhiṣiktaḥ*{612}* prakṣālipādapāṇir*{613}* apa ācamya surabhimatyā abliṅgābhir vāruṇībhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pāvamānībhiḥ vyāhṛtibhir anyaiś ca pavitrair ātmānaṃ prokṣya prayato bhavati. athāpy udāharanti." [BaudhDhS 2.4.7.1-3]
[73.18] "āpo 'vagāhanaṃ snānaṃ vihitaṃ sārvavarṇikam /
[73.19] mantravatprokṣaṇañ caiva dvijānām avaśiṣyate* //{614}*" iti [BaudhDhS 2.4.7.3-2]

[73.20-74.3] sarvakarmaṇāñ caivārambheṣu prāksandhyopāsanākālāc caitenaiva pavitrasamūhenātmānaṃ prokṣya prayato bhavati. athāpy udāharanti. "darbheṣv āsīno darbhān dhārayamāṇaḥ sodakapāṇinā*{615}* pratyaṅmukhaḥ sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtvaḥ āvartayet. prāṇāyāmaśo vā śatakṛtvaḥ. tribhiś ca prāṇāyāmaiḥ tato (tānto) brahmahṛdayena. vāruṇībhyāṃ rātrim upatiṣṭhate." ityādinā mārjanādikam uktam. pradhānabhūtam arghyapradānādikam anuktam. [BaudhDhS 2.4.7.4-9]

!{612}! BaudhDhS: vānabhiṣiktaḥ. !{613}! BaudhDhS: prakṣālitapādapāṇir. !{614}! BaudhDhS: mantravatprokṣaṇaṃ cāpi dvijātīnāṃ viśiṣyate. !{615}! BaudhDhS: sodakena pāṇinā.

[śrutyukto brahmayajñaprakāraḥ]

[brahmavaraṇapūrvakasomavaraṇam]

[74.4-9] brahmayajñaḥ. talavakāropaniṣadi "tasyā vā eṣa prathamaḥ pādaḥ oṃ bhūs tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ oṃ bhuvaḥ bhargo devasya dhīmahi oṃ suvaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt iti pacchaḥ, oṃ bhūr bhuvas tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi oṃ suvaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt ity ardhacaśaḥ, oṃ bhūrbhuvassuvas tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt iti samastāñ ca sāvitrīṃ japtveti yathodiṣṭaḥ, tathātra sūtre 'pi ukto 'sti.

[74.10-11] āghārādiṣu sarvam api śrautavat. atra brahmavaraṇānantaraṃ somavaraṇam apy uktam asti. "somo 'smākaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ rājā - somarājāno brāhmaṇā" iti.

[74.12-13] "viṣṇuś ca vai somaś ca brahmav ādyam avadetāṃ 'ahaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhe'ti viṣṇur abravīt 'ahaṃ pratiṣṭhe'ti somaḥ. tau prajāpatiṃ praśnam aitāṃ so 'bravīt prajāpatiḥ

[74.14] 'chandāṃsi viṣṇum adhigacchanti, nakṣatrāṇi somaṃ. tāv ubhau brahmaṇyāv'; iti so 'bravīt.

[74.15-17] pūjitau pūjayantau stutau stunvantau priyau priyavantau brahmaṇyau brahmavittau brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhātārau bhavata iti yan māṃ brahmaṇā vakṣyanti yajñeṣu so 'ham iti viṣṇur abravīt. tasmād viṣṇur yajño brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhā iti. vijñayate ca.

[74.18-22] "brāhmaṇo vai chandāṃsī"ty etasmāt brāhmaṇāt yan māṃ brāhmaṇā vakṣyanti nakṣatreṣu tatrāham iti so 'bravīt. tasmāt brāhmaṇānāṃ somo rājeti tasmād vijñāyate ca brāhmaṇe vā aṣṭāviṃśo nakṣatrāṇāṃ tasya vacaḥ puṇyam iti tāv ubhau brahmaṇyau brahmavittau brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhātārau brāhmaṇeṣu pratiṣṭhitau ya evaṃ brāhmaṇapuraskṛtāni karmāṇi karoti yajñasya samṛddhyā" iti ca śrutiprasiddhatvāt.

[74.23-25] evam atra śāntikapauṣṭikādiṣu pradhānakarmatvāt navagrahamakhasya pañcāgnikuṇḍavidhānam uktam. "atha grahaśāntiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. grahyāyattā lokayātrā tasmād ātmaviruddhe prāpte grahān samyak pūjayatī" ti.

[grahaśānteḥ prādhānyam]

[75.1-8] grahaśānteḥ kathaṃ prādhānyam iti ced ucyate. "udyantam astaṃyantam ādityam abhidhyāyan kurvan brāhmaṇo vidvān sakalaṃ bhadram aśnute 'sāv ādityo brahmeti brahmaiva san brahmāpy eti ya evaṃ veda" iti "ya eṣo 'ntarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣo dṛśyate" iti "yo 'sau tapann udeti" ityādi "viṣṇuśakter avasthānaṃ sadāditye karoti ca" iti "dhyeyas sadā savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartī" tyādibhiś ca vacanaiḥ yat pratipāditaṃ savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartino bhagavato nārāyaṇasya yajanaṃ tad evedam ity abhiprāyeṇa sūtrakārair asya grahayajñasya prādhānyam uktam. tathānte "anyathā mahattaro doṣo bhavatī"ty apy uktam.

[75.9] bodhāyanaś ca: "athāto grahātithyabalikarmopahārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ"

[savitṛhomaḥ]

[75.10] aśraddhadhānam aśucim ajapaṃ tyaktamaṅgalam /
[75.11] grahā nayanti suvyaktaṃ puruṣaṃ yamasādanam //

[75.12] grahāṇām ugraceṣṭānāṃ nakṣatrapathacāriṇām /
[75.13] upahārān pravakṣyāmi śāntyarthan tu yathāvidhi //"

[viṣṇvārādhanasya śrautatvam]

[75.14-16] māsi māsy ṛtāv ṛtau candragrahe sūryagrahe viṣuve 'yane śubhāśubhe janmanakṣatre tadgrahāṇām ātithyaṃ saṃvatsarād api prayuñjānaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnoti" iti grahaśāntikālaṃ nirūpya.
[75.17] "grahā gāvo narendrāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca viśeṣataḥ /
[75.18] pūjitāḥ pūjayanty enaṃ nirdahanty avamānitāḥ //"

[75.19] ity akaraṇe pratyavāyam api darśitavān.

[75.20-22] tasmād eva sūtrakāraiḥ sūryacandrau vinā lokapravṛtty asambhavāt sūryapradhānatvāc ca grahāṇāṃ sarvakarmaṇām ādau grahapuraskāram uktvā tatra pañcāgnikuṇḍavidhānam upadiśya pradhāne sabhye viṣṇurūpasya savituḥ homaḥ "sabhye savitur" iti pratipāditaḥ.

[75.23-24] evam - "nārāyaṇa paraṃ brahma" - "brahmaiva bhūtānāṃ jyeṣṭhāṃ tena ko 'rhati spardhitum" - "agnir vai devānām avamo viṣṇuḥ paramaḥ tadantareṇa sarvā anyā devatāḥ"

[śrutimūlakatve prāmāṇyātiśayaḥ]

[76.1] ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa "tasmād gṛhe paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sāyaṃprātarhomānte 'rcayati"

[76.2-3] iti nārāyaṇaparatvena sūtrāntareṣv anuktam ārādhanavidhim uktvā tatra "sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmā" ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa pañcamūrtividhānam apy uktam.

[76.4-5] āghārādiṣu śrautavad eveti pratyakṣasiddham iti pūrvam evoktam. evam anyatrāpi draṣṭavyam.

[76.6-7] śrutimārgānusāritve ko viśeṣa iti cet - ucyate. śrutimūlatve hi prāmāṇyātiśayasambhavaḥ. yathāha
[76.8] manu: "vedaḥ smṛtiḥ sadācāraḥ svasya ca priyam ātmanaḥ /
[76.9] etac catuṣṭayaṃ prāhuḥ*{616}* sākṣād dharmasya lakṣaṇam // [ManuDhŚ 2.12]

[76.10] sarvaṃ tu samavekṣyaitad akhilaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā*{617}* /
[76.11] śrutiprāmāṇyato vidvān svadharme niviśeta vai //" [ManuDhŚ 2.8]

[76.12] śrībhārate: "vedapraṇihito dharmo hy adharmas tadviparyayaḥ /
[76.13] vedo nārāyaṇas sākṣāt svayambhūr iti śuśrumaḥ //" [MBh ]

[76.14] pracetā: "amīṃāṃsyā bahiśśāstrā ye cānye vedabarjitaḥ /
[76.15] yattadbrūyur na tatkuryād vedād dharmo vidhīyate //"

[76.16] smṛtyantare: "dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ pramāṇaṃ prathamaṃ śrutiḥ / [MBh 14 App. 4.2492]

[76.17] dvitīyaṃ dharmaśāstrān tu*{618}* tṛtīyaṃ lokasaṅgrahaḥ* //{619}*" iti [MBh 14 App. 4.2493]

[76.18-20] etāvatā sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritva rūpaḥ tṛtīyo hetur nirūpito bhavati. tathā ca śrutimārgānusāritvād asya sūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ siddhyati iti nirūpitas tṛtīyo hetuḥ.

[76.21] iti tṛtīyahetunirūpaṇam.

!{616}! ManuDhŚ: etac caturvidhaṃ prāhuḥ. !{617}! ManuDhŚ: sarvaṃ tu samavekṣya-idaṃ nikhilaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā. !{618}! MBh: dharmaśāstrāṇi. !{619}! Dieser Vers ist auch als "Mahābhārata" zitiert in DHN[D] 93.17-18.

[caturthahetunirūpaṇam]

[vaikhānasasūtrasya samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvam]

[77.1-2] idānīṃ tāvat vaikhānasasūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānena anantasthiraphalaprāptiḥ satkulīnatvaṃ phalabhūyastvam api bhavatīti jñāpayituṃ "samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvād" iti caturtho hetu nirūpyate. tad yathā:

[77.4-10] atra sūtra*{620}* nityānuṣṭhānavidhau "indro 'ham ubhābhyām" ity ārabhya karaprakṣālanādīni samantrakatvenoktāni. brahmayajñe "ṛtañ ca satyañ ce" ty ādi viśeṣaḥ. puṇyāhe samantrakatvaṃ spaṣṭam. sūtrāntareṣv anuktam aupāsanāgnikuṇdavidhānaṃ pratipāditam. āghāravidhau samantrakatvaṃ siddham. antahome tathaiva. nāndīmukhapūrvakopanayanādiṣu śārīreṣu saṃskāreṣu samantrakatvaṃ pratyakṣam. sthālīpākādiṣu "pūrvavad" ity anena pūrvaṃ vistareṇa pratipāditasyāghāravidheḥ prayogasaukaryārthaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa pratipādanam.

[aparakriyāyām api samantrakatvam]

[77.11-15] aparakriyāyām apy asti samantrakatvam. tatra kvacit "tūṣṇīm" ity uktvatvāt samantrakatvaṃ nāstīti svayam evāśaṅkya prakārāntareṇa samantrakatvaṃ pratyapādayat. tatra tatra kvacit mantrayogyatābhāve 'pi vihitaviśaye sarvatra samantrakatvam astīty avagamyate. sūtrāntareṣu vihitaviśayeṣv api samantrakatvānukteḥ teṣāṃ samantrakasarvakriyātvaṃ nāsti. tatra aparakriyāyām api sūtrāntarānapekṣā dṛśyate.

[77.16-19] bodhāyanena agnimukhādiṣu paridhiparistaraṇādikṣepaṇam tūṣṇīm evoktam. samantrakatvena karmaṇām uktau ko viśeṣa iti cet - ucyate. karmaṇāṃ mantravattve hi vīryavattaratvaṃ karmārādhya bhagavatprīṇanadvārā anantasthiraphalaprāptiḥ satkulīnatvañ ca bhavantīti smṛtipurāṇādiṣv avagamyate. yathā

[karmaṇām samantrakatve vīryavattaratvam]

[77.20-22] chāndogye: "yad eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaniṣadā tad eva vīryavattaraṃ bhavatī"ti. tatraivaṃ vyākhyātam. "mantraprakāśitāni karmāṇi kriyante nāmantra kam asti karme"ti.

!{620}! Lies: sūtre.

[mantrahīnakarmanindā]

[78.1] ātharvaṇe: "ṛgyajussāmākhyā (?) mantreṣu karmāṇi kavayo yāny apaśyann iti"
[78.2] āraṇyaparvaṇi: "vratopanayanābhyāṃ vā upavāsena vā dvijaḥ /

[78.10] iti balicakravartinaṃ prati bhagavatā vāmanenoktam.

[78.19] ayājyayājanāc caiva nāstikyena ca karmaṇā*{627}* /
[78.20] kulāny akulatāṃ yānti yāni hīnāni mantrataḥ*{628}* // [ManuDhŚ 3.65]

[78.21] mantratas tu samṛddhāni kulāny alpadhanāni ca* /{629}*

[78.22] kulasaṃkhyāṃ ca gacchanti karṣanti ca mahad yaśaḥ* //{630}*" [ManuDhŚ 3.66]

[79.1] mantrapūtan tu yac chrāddham" iti somotpattau smaryate.

[pañcamahetunirūpaṇam; vaikhānasasūtrasya niṣekādisaṃskārapratipādakatvam]

[80.1] atha pañcamahetunirūpaṇam.

[80.2-5] athāsya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya sarvottamatve tatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇām api sarvotkṛṣṭatve ca itarasūtriṣu mukhyatvenānupapannaṃ niṣekādisaṃskārādimattvam*{631}* asya sūtrasya mukhyata evopapadyata iti jñāpayituṃ niṣekādisaṃskārādimatvād iti pañcamo hetur nirūpyate. yathā:

[saṃskāreṣu niṣekasya prathamatvam]

[80.6] "atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ, ṛtusaṅgamane"ty upakramya

[80.7] "pāṇigrahaṇānī"*{632}*ty antena śārīrasaṃskārā niṣekasaṃskārapūrvakatvena pratipāditāḥ.

[niṣekam antareṇa prajotpattyasaṃbhavaḥ]

[80.8-11] nanu: jātakopanayanavivāhānāntarabhāvino*{633}* niṣekasya katham āditvaṃ pratipādyate? tathā "brāhmaṇo 'sya mukham āsīt"*{634}* "manasā tv eva bhūtāni pūrvaṃ dakṣo 'sṛjat tadā" ityādi śrutismṛtiṣu niṣekena vinā utpattidarśanāc ca niṣekasya kim artham āditvaṃ pratipādyate? jātakasyāditvaṃ śrībhārate cāvagamyate.
[80.12] "jātakarmādibhir yais tu*{635}* saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaś śuciḥ /
[80.13] vedādhyayanasampannaṣ ṣaṭsu karmasv avasthitaḥ // [MB.h 12.182.2]

[80.14] śaucācāraratas samyak bhikṣārthī ca gurupriyaḥ*{636}* /
[80.15] nityavratas*{637}* satyaparaḥ sa vai brāhmaṇa ucyate //" iti [MBh 12.182.3]

[80.16] evaṃ harivaṃśe: *{638}*"kva dārāḥ kva ca saṃsargaḥ*{639}* kva ca bhāvaviparyayaḥ /
[80.17] yadiyaṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā // [HariV 35.42]

[80.18] yady asti tapaso vīryaṃ yuṣmākaṃ viditātmanāṃ*{640}* /
[80.19] sṛjadhvaṃ mānasān putrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā //" [HariV 35.43]

[80.20] iti niṣekaṃ vināpi utpattiḥ śrūyate iti niṣekasyāditvaṃ na saṃbhavati iti cet -

[80.21-23] tad asat. "niṣekavirahe 'pi utpattis saṃbhavatī"ty etan nopapadyate. tapobalād yogabalāc ca bhagavato nārāyaṇasya brahmaṇo maharṣīṇāṃ vā mānasaprajāsṛṣṭau śaktis sambhavati. nānyeṣām. yathā:*{641}*

Bezug auf VaikhSmS 1.1: atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. ṛtusaṃgamanagarbhādhānapuṃsavanasīmantaviṣṇubalijātakarmutthānanāmakaraṇānnaprāśanapravāsāgamanapiṇḍavardhanacauḍakopanayanapārāyaṇavratabandhavisargopākarmasamāvartanapāṇigrahaṇānīty aṣṭādaśa saṃskārāḥ śārīrāḥ. !{633}! MBh: śaucācārasthitaḥ samyag [die Lesart DHN[D] ist jedoch v.l.] vighasāśī gurupriyaḥ /. !{637}! MBh: nityavratī. !{638}! DHN[T] 389 ins. jaurvaḥ. !{639}! HariV: saṃyogaḥ. !{640}! [81.1] śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "saṅkalpād darśanāt sparśāt pūrveṣām abhavan prajāḥ" [ViṣṇuP ]

[81.2] tapoviṣeśair iddhānāṃ tadātyantatapasvinām* //{642}*" [ViṣṇuP 1.15.79]

[81.5] kāniṣṭhyaṃ śryaiṣṭhyam apy eṣāṃ pūrvaṃ nāsti dvijottama* //{643}* [ViṣṇuP 1.15.84ab]

[niṣekakriyāprakāraḥ]

[81.23] yadā 'sya sṛjamānasya na vyavardhanta tāḥ prajāḥ /
