ViṣṇuP: tataḥ saṃcinty sa punaḥ sṛṣṭihetoḥ prajāpatiḥ.

[82.1] maithunenaiva dharmeṇa sisṛkṣur vividhāḥ prajāḥ /
[82.2] tataḥ prabhṛti maitreya prajā maithunasambhavāḥ //" [ViṣṇuP 1.15.79ab?]

[82.3] bhārate: "na caiṣāṃ maithuno dharmo babhūva bharatarṣabha /
[82.4] saṅkalpād eva caiteṣāṃ garbhas samupapadyate* //{658}* [MBh 12.200.35]

[82.5] tatra tretāyuge kāle saṃsparśāj jāyate prajā* /{659}*

[82.6] na hy abhūn maithuno dharmas teṣām api narādhipa*{660}* // [MB.h 12.200.36]

[82.7] dvāpare maithuno dharmaḥ prajānām abhavan nṛpa /
[82.8] tathā kaliyuge kāle*{661}* dvandvam āpedire janāḥ //" iti [MBh 12.200.37]

[82.9-10] evaṃ śrutismṛtiṣu sṛṣṭikālād ārabhya niṣekād evotpar*{662}* iti śravaṇāt niṣekena vinā utpādanasāmarthyābhāvāc ca niṣekādimatvād ity uktam.*{663}*

[niṣekaśabdārthanirṇayaḥ]

[82.11-13] atrāpastambīyā evam āhuḥ. "niṣeko nāma garbhādhānam eva, niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ paryāyatvāt garbhādhānātirekeṇa niṣekaśabdasyārthāntarāsambhavāc ca.*{664}* garbhādhānaśabdasyārthe vicāryamāṇe 'garbho 'sminn ādhīyate'*{665}* iti vyutpattyā 'indriyaṃ vai garbha'*{666}*

[82.14-15] iti śrutyanusāreṇa retassecanam eva garbhādhānam ity avagateḥ*{667}* niṣekāditvam asmākam apy astī"ti.

[82.16-19] atra baudhāyanīyaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhante. "yad uktaṃ 'niṣeko nāma garbhādhānam niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ paryāyatvād'; iti - tadasat. niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ pṛthaktvena pratipādanāt paryāyatvaṃ na ghaṭate. yathā - 'caturthyāṃ snātāyāṃ niśāyām alaṅkṛtya śayane 'bhimantrayate 'viṣṇur yonim'; ity upakramya 'athainām upaiti'; - 'tvāṃ pūṣann ...'*{668}* iti.

[82.20-23] evaṃ niṣeka uktaḥ. 'atha garbhādhānavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ*{669}* vācayitvā atha devayajanaprabhṛtyāgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti - pravedhase kavaye medhyāye'*{670}*ti. iti garbhādhānam uktam. evaṃ niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ pṛthaktvena kīrtanāt*{671}* niṣeka eva garbhādhānam iti vaktum ayuktam.

[82.24-25] kiñca āpastambasūtre*{672}* niṣekapūrvakatvenānuktatvāt catvāriṃśat saṃskāraparigaṇane agṛhītatvāc ca teṣāṃ niṣekādyās saṃskārā na bhavantīti.*{673}*"

!{658}! MBh: apatyam udapadyata; die Lesart des DHN[D] ist als v.l. angegeben; DHN[T] 396: garbhasamupapadyate. !{659}! MBh: saṃkalpājñāyate prajā. !{660}! MBh: janādhipa; DHN[D] ist v.l. !{661}! MBh: tathā kaliyuge rājan. !{662}! Lies: evotpattir. !{663}! DHN[T] 396-397 statt DHN[D] 82.9-10: atra śrutismṛtiṣu sṛṣṭikālād ārabhya niṣekād evotpattir iti śrūyamāṇatvāt niṣekena vinotpādanasāmarthyābhāvāc ca niṣekāditvenoktam. !{664}! DHN[T] 396: *bhvād garbhā. !{665}! Vgl. NVB 1.1: garbhaḥ ādhīyate anenāsyām iti garbhādhānam. !{666}! Vgl. DHN[D] 81.14 und 84.15: indriyam garbho. !{667}! DHN[T] 397: ato statt avagateḥ. !{668}! Bezug auf BaudhGṛS 1.7.37-44: caturtyāṃ snātāyāṃ niśāyām alaṅkṛtya śayane 'bhimantrayate viṣṇur yoniṃ kalpayatu tvaṣṭā rūpāṇi piṃśatu. āsiñ catuprajāpatir dhātā garbhaṃ dadhātu te (37). yathāgnigarbhā pṛthivī dyauryathendreṇa garbhiṇī. vāyur yathā diśāṃ garbha evaṃ garbhaṃ dadhātu te (38). garbhaṃ dhehi sinīvālī garbhaṃ dhehi sarasvati. garbhaṃ te aśvinau devāv āghāttāṃ puṣkarasrajā (39). hiraṇyayī araṇī yaṃ nirmanthato aśvinā. taṃ te garbhaṃ dadhāmy ahaṃ daśame māsi sūtave (40). nejam eṣa parāpata saputraḥ punar āpataḥ. asyai me putrakāmāyai garbham ādhehi yaḥ pumān. iti (41). athaināṃ pariṣvajati amūham asmi sā tvaṃ dyaur ahaṃ pṛthivī tvaṃ reto 'haṃ retibhṛt tvaṃ mano 'ham asmi vā tvaṃ sāmāham asmi ṛktvaṃ tāvehi sambhavāva saha reto dadhāvahai puṃse putrāya vettavai rāyaspoṣāya suprajāstvāya suvīryāya iti (42). ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśate ahaṃ garbham adadhām oṣadhīṣv ahaṃ viśveṣu bhuvaneṣv antaḥ. ahaṃ prajā ajanayanpitṛṇām ahaṃ janibhyo aparīṣu putrān iti (43). athainām upaiti tāṃ pūṣañchvitamomarayasva yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyā vapanti. yā na ūrū uśatī visrayātai yasyām uśantaḥ praharema śepham iti (44); s.a. DHN[D] 83.5. !{669}! DHN[T] 400 ins. in Übereinstimmung mit BaudhGṛŚeṣS: svastim ṛddhim iti. !{670}! Bezug auf BaudhGṛŚeṣS 2.2.1: atha garbhādhānaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ svasty ṛddhim iti vācayitvātha devayajanollekhanaprabhṛtyāgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakkāj juhoti: pravedhase kavaye medhyāya vaco vandāru vṛṣabhāya vṛṣṇe ... !{671}! DHN[T] 400: vidyamānatvān. !{672}! DHN[T] 401 om. āpastambasūtre. !{673}! DHN[T] 401: saṃskāreṣu (na) agṛhītatvān niṣekaśabdasmaraṇābhāvāc ca yuṣṃākaṃ niṣekādyasaṃskārā na bhavantīty statt saṃskāraparigaṇane agṛhītatvāc ca teṣāṃ niṣekādyās saṃskārā na bhavantīti.

[83.1-6] atra āpastambīyā ūcuḥ. "yady asmākaṃ niṣekādyāḥ saṃskārā na bhavantīty ucyate tarhi yuṣmākam api tathaiva, bhavat sūtre 'pi*{674}* >yato etad dhutaḥ prahutaḥ*{675}* āhutaḥ śūlagavo baliharaṇaṃ pratyavarohaṇam aṣṭakā pārvaṇahoma itī

<*{676}*ty ārabhya vivāhādyevoktam - na tu niṣekāditvena. kiñca sūtropakrame*{677}* saṃskāragaṇanāyām api niṣekas tu saṃskāratvena vā śabdamātreṇa vā na pratipāditaḥ. kiñca >caturyyāṃ snātāyom<*{678}* ityādinā pṛthaktvena vidhīyamānasya garbhādhānasya lakṣaṇapratipādanābhāvāt viśiṣya kālanirūpaṇābhāvāc ca.*{679}*>

[vaikhānasānām eva niṣekādisaṃskāravattvam]

[83.7] (vaikhānase sūtre eva niṣekāditvena uktatvāc ca vaikhānasānām niṣekāditvam),

[83.8] āvayoḥ*{680}* ubhayor api niṣekādyās saṃskārā na bhavanti iti. ayam eva siddhāntaḥ.*{681}*

[itareṣāṃ garbhadhānādisaṃskāravattvam]

[83.9] tathā ca: "niṣekādyāḥ śmaśānāntās teṣāṃ vai mantrataḥ kriyāḥ / [YājñavalkyaDhŚ 1.10cd]

[83.10] garbhādhānam ṛtau puṃsasavanaṃ spandānāt purā* //{682}*" [YājñavalkyaDhŚ 1.11ab]

[83.11-14] iti yājñavalkyoktau teṣām iti śabdena "mukhye sambhavaty amukhyakalpanāyogād" iti nyāyena mukhyatvena śrīvaikhānasasūtre eva niṣekāditvasya vidyamānatvāt vaikhānasā eva parāmṛśyante iti - teṣām eva niṣekāditvam, itareṣāṃ niṣekāditvaṃ na sambhavati. api tu garbhādhānāditvam eva. ayam eva yājñavalkyābhiprāyaḥ.*{683}*

[83.15-20] athocyete*{684}*. garbhādhānalakṣaṇam anuktaṃ viśiṣya kālaś cānukta iti yad uktam tatrocyate - sarveṣāṃ kāraṇabhūtena paramācāryeṇa vikhanasā praṇīte śrīvaikhānasasūtre "atha gṛhītagarbhāliṅgāni śarīrāṭopaḥ sakthisīdanaṃ dveṣo bhartur arucir āhāre lālāprakopaḥ kharatā vācaḥ sphuraṇaṃ yoner iti garbhasya daivānubandhaṃ jñātvā āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye punnāmni śubhe nakṣatre"*{685}* ityādinā garbhādhānalakṣaṇakālayor api vaikhānasasūtre pratipāditvāt:*{686}*
[83.21] "vede vaikhānase sūtre yo dharmaḥ parikīrtitaḥ /
[83.22] sarvaiḥ sa dharmo 'nuṣṭheyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā* //{687}*"

[83.23] iti bhṛguṇoktatvāt "anuktam*{688}* anyato grāhyam" iti nyāyāt vikhanasaḥ*{689}* ācāryatvena

[83.24-25] bhāratādiṣu pratipāditavyāc ca "anuktāṃśeṣu vaikhānasoktaprakāreṇa asmābhir api kartuṃ yuktam" iti. etad eva yuktataram. Tathāhi:*{690}*

[niṣekagarbhādhānayor aparyāyatvam]

[84.1-10] āpastambādīnām ācāryeṇa bodhāyanena svaśiṣyān prati*{691}* "athātra pākayajñānāṃ prāyaścittir" ity ārabhya "vyāhṛtīnāṃ prayoge ayathākṛtaṃ yathākṛtaṃ*{692}* bhavatīty ācāryā bruvate. tatrāpy udāharanti"*{693}* iti, "caturthīprabhṛtyā ṣoḍaśīm uttarām uttarām*{694}* upaiti. prajāniḥśreyasam ṛtugamanam ity ācāryāḥ. sarvāṇy upagamanāni mantravanti bhavantīti bodhāyanaḥ. yac cādau yac cartāv iti śālīkir"*{695}* iti - "athāsyātithayo bhavanti guros samānavṛttir vaikhānasaḥ snātako rājā vā dharmayuktaḥ. teṣām abhyutthāyāsanaṃ pādyam arhaṇam arghyaṃ vā prajuñjīta"*{696}* iti - "ekam agnihotraṃ sāyam upakramaṃ prātar apavargam ācāryā bruvate tatrodāharanti" iti, "vaikhānasānāṃ na druhyet" ityādi sūtreṣu "ācāryā bruvate" iti nirdiṣṭaḥ ācāryaḥ vaikhānasa eveti vaktuṃ yuktam*{697}* - manvādīnāṃ śārīrasaṃskāravaktṛtvābhāvāt, bodhāyanena pratipāditasya vaikhānasasūtre vidyamānatvāt,

[84.11] "guroḥ samānavṛttir vaikhānasaḥ"*{698}* iti bodhāyanenaivoktatvāt, "vikhanasācārye"ti.*{699}*

[84.12-13] bhārate pratipāditvāc ca. tathā ca sarveṣāṃ kāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvāt tatsūtroktaprakāreṇa sarvaiḥ*{700}* kartuṃ yuktam eva. kiñca araṇyādipātralakṣaṇam api tatraiva pratipāditam.

[84.14] anye 'py āhuḥ. "asmākam api niṣekāditvaṃ*{701}* samānam" iti. tad apy asat.

[84.15] garbhādhānaśabdasyārthe vicāryamāṇe "yoniṃ praviśad indriyaṃ garbho jarāyuṇā vṛta"*{702}* iti

[84.16-20] pramāṇena garbhagole praviṣṭasya retasa eva garbhaśabdavācyatvam avagamyate. na tv itarasya kevala retasaḥ. tathā - "āsiñcatu prajāpatir dhātā garbhaṃ dadhātu" iti niṣekakriyānantarabhāvitvāt garbhādhānasya, niṣekasya tu pratyārtavaṃ kartuṃ vyogyatāsambhavāt adhṛtaretasaḥ srāvadoṣaprasaṅgāt śrutismṛtivirodhāt pratyakṣavirodhāṅ ca niṣeka eva garbhādhānam iti vaktum ayuktam.*{703}*

[84.22] śrotriyatvaṃ dharmaśāstrādhikāritvaṃ brahmaśarīritvañ*{705}* ca bodhāyanādibhir uktam. yathā:

[85.7-8] atra manuvākye "yasya - tasya - kasyacit" ityādi śabdānāṃ vaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt "sarveṣāṃ niṣekāditvaṃ samānam" iti vaktum ayuktam.

[85.9] āśvamedhike bhagavān: "vaidikaiḥ karmabhiḥ puṇyaiḥ niṣekādir dvijanmanām* /{711}*

[85.10] kāryaḥ śarīrasaṃskāraḥ pāvanaḥ pretya ceha ca // [MB.h 14, App. 4.2513]

[85.11] gārbhair homair jātakarma*{712}*nāmacaulopanāyanaiḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.2514]

[85.12] svādhyāyaiś ca tapobhiś ca*{713}* vivāhasnātakavrataiḥ // [MBh 14, App. 4.2515]

[85.13] mahāyajñaiś ca yajñaiś ca brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥ /" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.2516]

[85.14] evam anyatrāpi draṣṭavyam.

[85.15] bodhāyanena "yato etad dhutam*{714}*" ityādinā sūtrādau vivāhapūrvakatvenoktam.

[85.16-21] āpastambena "atha karmāṇy ācārādyāni gṛhyante*{715}*" ity ārabhya "upanayanaṃ vyākhyāsyāma" iti. bhāradvājasatyāṣāḍhābhyām āśvalāyanena ca "uktāni vaitānikānī"*{716}*ty ārabhya vaiśvadevapūrvakatvena. drāhyāyaṇena*{717}* "athāto gṛhyakarmāṇi, udagayanapūrvapakṣa"*{718}* ity ārabhya ācārāditvena. kātyāyanaś ca "athāto gṛhyasthālīpākānāṃ karme"*{719}*ty ārabhya pratipāditavān. "atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāma"*{720}* ity ārabhya niṣekapūrvakatvena bhagavatā vikhanasaiva*{721}* pratipāditam.

[85.22-24] evaṃ ca niṣekapūrvakatvenoktatvād*{722}* asya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānenaiva tatsūtriṇāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭatvañ copapadyate iti śrutismṛtipurāṇādimukhena pratipāditam iti nirūpitaḥ pañcamo hetuḥ.

[85.25] iti pañcamahetunirūpaṇam

!{707}! DHN[T] 413: mantravatsamprayoge tau. !{708}! DHN[T] 413: niṣekādiś. !{709}! Dieser Vers ist auch in DHN[D] 83.9-10 zitiert; DHN[T] 413 ins. (bahir iti). !{710}! DHN[T] 413 mit ManuDhŚ: mantrair yasyodito vidhiḥ. !{711}! MBh 14, App. 4.2512. !{712}! MBh: garbhahomair jātakarma. !{713}! MBh: svādhyāyais tadvrataiś caiva. !{714}! Bezug auf BaudhGṛS 1.1.1, auch in DHN[D] 83.1-3 zitiert (s.o.). DHN[T] 414 : dhuta. !{715}! DHN[T] 414: karmaṇyācārādhyāni gṛhyanta. !{716}! Bezug auf ĀśvalāyanaGṛS 1.1.1: uktāni vaitānikāni gṛhyāni vakṣyāmaḥ. !{717}! DHN[T] 415: drāhyāyaṇena. !{718}! Drāhyāyaṇagṛhyasūtra? !{719}! Kātyāyanagṛhyasūtra? !{720}! Bezug auf VaikhSmS 1.1 (s.o.). !{721}! DHN[T] 416: vikhanasā. !{722}! Vgl. DHN[D] 2.7: niṣekasaṃskārādimatvāt.

[ṣaṣṭhahetunirūpaṇam]

[vaikhānasasūtrasyāṣṭādaśasaṃskārapratipādakatvam]

[86.1] atha ṣaṣṭhahetunirūpaṇam

[86.2-4] athedānīṃ śrīvaikhānasasūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇām eva sarvebhyaḥ śreṣṭhamatvaṃ sūtrāntareṣv anuktaṃ śrutisiddhāṣṭādaśasaṃskāravatvaṃ kriyābāhulyañ ca sambhavatīti jñāpayituṃ "aṣṭādaśasaṃskārapratipādakatvād" iti ṣaṣṭho hetur nirūpyate. tathā hi:

[86.5-8] "atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ṛtusaṅgamana-garbādhāna-puṃsavana-sīmanta-viṣṇubali-jātakarmotthāna-nāmakaraṇānnaprāśana-pravāsāgamana-piṇḍavardhana-caulopanayana-pārāyaṇa-vratabandhavisargopākarma-samāvartana-pāṇigrahaṇānīty aṣṭādaśa-saṃskārāś śārīrāḥ"*{723}* iti aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāḥ sūtre pratipāditāḥ. ete ca

["aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ yeṣu karme" ti śrutyarthavicāraḥ]

[86.9-10] śrutisiddhāḥ. yathā muṇḍopaniṣadi - "plavā hy ete adṛḍhā yajñarūpā aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ yeṣu karma. etac chreyo ye 'bhinandanti mūḍhā jarāmṛtyuṃ te punar evāpi yanti"*{724}* iti.

[86.11] atra kecid evam ūcuḥ: "yajñasya rtvijaṣ ṣoḍaśa sadasyassaptadaśaḥ yajamāno 'ṣṭādaśaḥ"

[86.12-14] iti śrutyanusāreṇa "aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ yeṣu karme"*{725}*ty atra yajamānādaya eva vivakṣitā iti. tad asat. "aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ karmayeṣu" ity uktatvāt. ṛtvigyajamānādayo hi yāgakartāraḥ na tu karma. "yeṣu" ity asya padasya yeṣu sūtreṣv ity arthaḥ.

[86.15-18] 'avaraṃ karma'; jātakādayaḥ, smārtakarmatvāt. ātmaguṇarahitā yāgadayaḥ jātakarmādayaś ca. 'adṛḍhāḥ plavāḥ'; saṃsārottārakā na bhavanti. tathā ca atra adṛḍhaplavatvena ninditā saṃskārāḥ yāgādayaś ca ātmaguṇarahitā eva vivakṣitāḥ. tat sahitānāṃ teṣāṃ mokṣasādhakatvam. yathā:

[ātmaguṇarahitānāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ bandhakatvam]

[86.19-21] gautamadharme: "yasya tu khalu catvāriṃśatsaṃskārā na cāṣṭāvātmaguṇāḥ na sa brahmaṇas sāyujyaṃ sālokyañ ca gacchati. yasya khalu catvāriṃśatsaṃskārāṇām ekadeśo py aṣṭāv ātmaṇāḥ atha sa brahmaṇas sāyujyaṃ sālokyañ ca gacchati gacchatī"*{726}*ti.

[aṣṭānām ātmaguṇānāṃ lakṣaṇāni]

[86.22-23] 'aṣṭāv ātmaguṇāḥ': "dayā samastabhūteṣu kṣāntir anasūyā śaucam anāyāso maṅgalyam akārpaṇyam aspṛhe"*{727}* ti. tallakṣaṇāni tu:

[tatra dayālakṣaṇaṃ]

[86.24] "abandhau bandhuvarge vā mitre dveṣṭari vā tathā /
[86.25] āpanne rakṣaṇaṃ yat tu dayaiṣā parikīrtitā //

!{723}! VaikhSmS 1.1. !{724}! MuṇḍakaU 1.2.7: plavā hy ete adṛḍhā yajñarūpā aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ yeṣu karma. etac chreyo ye 'bhinandanti mūḍhā jarāmṛtyuṃ te punar evāpiyanti. !{725}! MuṇḍakaU 1.2.7. !{726}! Bezug auf GautamaDhS 1.8.25(8.24): yasyaite catvāriṃśatsaṃskārā na caāṣṭāv ātmaguṇā na sa brahmaṇaḥ sāyujyaṃ sālokyaṃ gacchati / und GautamaDhS 1.8.26(8.25): yasya tu khalu catvāriṃśataṃskārāṇām ekadeśo 'py aṣṭāv ātmaguṇā atha sa brahmaṇaḥ sāyujyaṃ sālokyaṃ ca gacchati. !{727}! Bezug auf GautamaDhS 1.8.24(8.23): dayā sarvabhūteṣu kṣāntir anasūyā śaucam anāyāso maṅgalam akārpaṇyam aspṛheti.

[tatra kṣamālakṣaṇam]

[87.1] bāhye vā 'bhyantare vāpi duḥkha utpādite paraiḥ /
[87.2] na prakupyati no hanti sā kṣamā parikīrtitā //

[tatra anasūyālakṣaṇam]

[87.3] saguṇān guṇi*{728}* no hanti (?) stauti mandaguṇān api /
[87.4] nānyadoṣeṣu ramate sā 'nasūyā prakīrtitā //

[tatra śaucalakṣaṇam]

[87.5] abhakṣyaparihāraś ca saṃsargaś cāpy aninditaiḥ /
[87.6] svadharme ca vyavasthānaṃ śaucam etad udāhṛtam //

[tatra anāyāsalakṣaṇam]

[87.7] śarīraṃ pīḍyate yena suśubhenāpi karmaṇā /
[87.8] atyantaṃ tannakartavyam anāyāsas sa ucyate //

[tatra maṅgalyalakṣaṇam]

[87.9] praśastācaraṇaṃ nityam apraśastavisarjanam /
[87.10] etad dhi maṅgalaṃ proktam ṛṣibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ //

[tatra akārpaṇyalakṣaṇam]

[87.11] stokād api pradātavyam adīnenāntarātmanā /
[87.12] ahanyahani yatkiñcid akārpaṇyaṃ tad ucyate //

[tatra aspṛhālakṣaṇam]

[87.13] yathotpanneṣu santoṣaḥ kartavyas svāgatair dhanaiḥ /
[87.14] parārthān nābhibhāṣeta sā 'spṛhā parikīrtitā //" iti

[87.15] prasaṅgād idam uktam. prakṛtam anusarāmaḥ.

[sāttvikarājasatāmasapurāṇāni]

[87.16-17] atha aṣṭādaśasmṛtyuktāni aṣṭādaśapurāṇeṣūktānīti vā muṇḍakaśrutyartho 'stu iti cet. tad apy asat. smṛtipurāṇādiṣu aṣṭādaśakarmeti viśiṣyānuktatvāt.

[87.18-20] atra *{729}* "aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ karma yeṣv"*{730}* iti sāmānyenoktatvāt tatroktānāṃ yogādīnām apy apavargaprāpakatvābhāvāt punar api jarāmṛtyuprāpakatvāc ca na smṛtipurāṇeṣūktānīti vaktuṃ yuktaṃ kiñ ca
[87.21] pādmapurāṇe: "vaiṣṇavaḥ*{731}* nāradīyañ ca tathā bhāgavataṃ śubhaṃ /
[87.22] gāruḍañ ca tathā pādmaṃ vārāhaṃ śubhadarśane // [Padma.P uttarabhāga 236.19]

!{728}! Lies: guṇī. !{729}! Anm. des Herausgebers: atra aṣṭādaśapurāṇeṣu smṛtiṣu coktānāṃ śrautasmārtakarmaṇām eva avaram iti paryudāso na paryāptaḥ. tatroktayogādīnām api keṣāñcit jīrṇaplavatvasya siddhatvād iti bhāvaḥ. !{730}! MuṇḍakaU 1.2.7. !{731}! PadmaP: vaiṣṇavaṃ.

[sātvikapurāṇaśraiṣṭhyam]

[88.1] sāttvikāni purāṇāni vijñeyāni ca ṣaṭ pṛthak* /{732}*

[88.2] brahmāṇḍaṃ brahmakaivartaṃ*{733}* mārkaṇḍeyaṃ tathaiva ca // [Padma.P uttarabhāga 236.20]

[88.3] bhaviṣyad vāmanaṃ brāhmaṃ rājasāni ca ṣaḍvidhāḥ*{734}* / [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.21ab]

[88.4] mātsyaṃ kaurmaṃ tathā laiṅgaṃ śaivaṃ skāndaṃ tathaiva ca /
[88.5] āgneyañ ca ṣaḍ etāni tāmasāni nibodha me //" iti [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.18]

[88.6] mātsye: "saṅkīrṇās tāmasāś caiva rājasās sāttvikās tathā /
[88.7] kalpāś caturvidhāḥ proktāḥ brahmaṇo divasāś ca te /
[88.8] yasmin kalpe tu yatproktaṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā purā // [MatsyaP]

[88.9] tasya tasya tu māhātmyaṃ tena rūpeṇa vartate /
[88.10] saṅkīrṇeṣu sarasvatyāḥ pitṝṇāñ ca nigadyate // [MatsyaP]

[88.11] agneś śivasya māhātmyaṃ tāmaseṣu prakīrtyate /
[88.12] rājaseṣu tu māhātmyam adhikaṃ brahmaṇo viduḥ // [MatsyaP]

[88.13] sāttvikeṣv atha kalpeṣu māhātmyam adhikaṃ hareḥ /
[88.14] teṣv eva yogasaṃsiddhā gamiṣyanti parāṃ gatiṃ //" iti [MatsyaP]

[88.15] pādme: "vāsiṣṭhañ caiva hārītaṃ vyāsaṃ pārāśaraṃ tathā // [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.23cd]

[88.16] bhāradvājaṃ kāśyapīyaṃ smṛtiṣaṭkantu sāttvikam /
[88.17] mānavaṃ yajñavalkyañ ca ātreyaṃ dākṣyam eva ca* //{735}* [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.24]

[88.18] kātyāyanaṃ vaiṣṇavañ ca smṛtiṣaṭkantu rājasam /
[88.19] gautamaṃ bārhaspatyañ ca sāṃvartañ ca yamasmṛtiḥ* //{736}* [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.25]

[88.20] śāmbham auśanasañ caiva smṛtiṣaṭkantu tāmasam* //{737}*" iti [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.26ab]

[88.21] tathā: "sāttvikā mokṣadā jñeyā rājasāḥ svargadāḥ smṛtāḥ* /{738}* [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.21cd]

[88.22] tathaiva tāmasā devi nirayaprāptihetavaḥ //" [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.22ab]

[88.23-24] ityādi vacanasiddhasātvikapurāṇeṣu pratipāditānāṃ bhagavadārādhanādīnāṃ mokṣahetutvasmaraṇāt, sāmanyena aṣṭādaśapurāṇoktakarmaṇāṃ jīrṇaplavasādṛśyaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyam.

!{732}! PadmaP: sāttvikāni purāṇāni vijñeyāni śubhāni vai. !{733}! PadmaP: brahmāṇḍaṃ brahmavaivarttaṃ. !{734}! PadmaP: bhaviṣyaṃ vāmanaṃ brāhmaṃ rājasāni nibodha me. !{735}! PadmaP: bhāradvājaṃ kāśyapaṃ ca sātvikā muktidāḥ śubhāḥ / yajñavalkyaṃ tathātreyaṃ taittiriṃ dākṣam eva ca. !{736}! PadmaP: kātyāyanaṃ vaiṣṇavañ ca rājasāḥ svargadāḥ śubhāḥ / gautamaṃ bārhaspatyañ ca sāṃvartañ ca yamasmṛtam. !{737}! PadmaP: śāṅkhyaṃ cauśanasañ ceti tāmasā nirayapradāḥ. !{738}! PadmaP: sāttvikā mokṣadāḥ proktā rājasāḥ sarvadā śubhāḥ; vgl. PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.25b: rājasāḥ svargadāḥ śubhāḥ.

[vaikhānase kriyābāhulyam]

[89.1-2] anyathā svargamokṣanirayāṇām ekarūpatvāṅgīkārāpātāt. ataḥ śrīmadvaikhānasasūtroktāṣṭādaśasaṃskārā evety avagantavyam. bodhāyanasūtre saṃskārasaṅkhyā na kṛtā.

[89.3-5] āpastambādināpi pañcamahāyajñānāṃ nityahomasya ca pākayajñatvenāṅgīkārāt ete ṣoḍasaṃskārā iti vivicyānuktatvāt aparasaṃskārapratipādanābhāvāc ca na tatroktāḥ gṛhītuṃ śakyāḥ.

[89.6-8] śrīvaikhānase tu kriyābāhulyam apy asti. tathā hi. aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāḥ pākayajñāś ca pṛthaktvenopapaditāḥ. varṣavardhanādyāstu viśeṣāḥ. pañcamahāyajñasahitā dvāviṃśadyajñāḥ - pañcamahāyajñānām ekatvam. aparaś cāṣṭādaśavyatirikta iti.

[89.9] kriyābāhulyena kim ādhikyam iti cet - ucyate. muṇḍopaniṣadi -

[89.10] "kriyāvān eṣa brahmavidāṃ variṣṭhaḥ*{739}*" iti "kriyāvantaḥ śrotriyā brahmaṇiṣṭhāḥ svayaṃ juhvata

[89.11] ekarṣiṃ śraddhayantaḥ. teṣām evaitāṃ brahmavidyāṃ vadeta*{740}*" iti ca śrūyate.

[89.12-15] bodhāyanaḥ: "tasmād yaḥ kaścana kriyāvān satām anumatācāras sa śrotriyas sa eva vijñeyas sa eva vijñeyaḥ" iti. kiñca - karmabhūyastvāt phalabhūyastvañ ca "yathopāsanaṃ phalam" iti nyāyāt siddhyati. ataḥ: aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāpratipādakatvād asya sūtrasya śreṣṭḥatvaṃ etas sūtriṇāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭatvañ copapadyata iti nirūpitaḥ ṣaṣṭho hetuḥ.

[89.16] iti ṣaṣṭhahetunirūpaṇam.

!{739}! Bezug auf MuṇḍakaU 3.1.4: prāṇo hy eṣa yaḥ sarvabhūtair vibhāti vijānan vidvān bhavate nātivādī. ātmakrīḍa ātmaratiḥ kriyāvān eṣa brahmavidāṃ variṣṭhaḥ. !{740}! Bezug auf MuṇḍakaU 3.2.10: tad etad ṛcābhyuktam. kriyāvantaḥ śrotriyā brahmaniṣṭhāḥ svayaṃ juhvata ekarṣiṃ śraddhayantaḥ. teṣām evaitāṃ brahmavidyāṃ vadeta śirovrataṃ vidhivad yais tu cīrṇam.

[saptamahetunirūpaṇam]

[90.1-3] atha śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya itarasūtrāpekṣābhāvāt svātantryam astīti jñāpayituṃ sāṅgakriyākalāpavattvād iti saptamo hetur nirūpyate. tathā hi: atrasūtre aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāḥ śārīrāḥ prasiddhās sāṅgāḥ eva pratipāditāḥ.

[90.4-8] nanu - aṅkurārpaṇaśatābhiṣekāgnidvayasaṃsargaputraparigrahabrahmamedhavṛṣotsarjanādipratipādanābhavāt sāṅgakriyākalāpavattvaṃ nāstīti cet - tad asat. iyaṃ śaṅkā śrīvaikhānasasūtrasvarūpānabhijñatvakṛtā. idaṃ sūtram ekādaśapraśnātmakam. atra na pratipāditānīti uktiḥ, atiriktatvena gṛhyapariśiṣṭasadbhāvājñānāt. gṛhyapariśiṣṭasadbhāvaḥ katham avagamyate iti cet - ucyate.

[90.9] "athāṅkurārpaṇavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ" ity ārabhya khaṇḍadvayenāṅkurārpaṇam uktam.
[90.10-11] "sāyaṃ sthaṇḍile sahasraṃ piṣṭena somarūpāṇi karotī"ty atra viśeṣeṇa sthaṇḍilādipratipādanam.
[90.12] "śatābhiṣekaṃ pūrvāhṇe puṇyāhaṃ dvijabhojanam* //{741}*" ity ārabhya [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]

[90.13] "sāyaṃ gomayasaṃlipte sthaṇḍile prāg anunnate /
[90.14] prācīrekhā dvipañcāśat saṃkhyayā tatra saṃlikhet // [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS.]

[90.15] udīcīś ca tathā rekhā dvatriṃśatsaṃkhyayā*{742}* likhet*{743}* //" [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]

[90.16] ityādinā śatābhiṣekaprayogaś ca uktaḥ.

[90.17] tathā "dhautavastradhāriṇau syātām" ity ārabhya [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[90.18] "dīpādyalaṅkṛte gehe vrīhīn āstīrya tatra vai /
[90.19] carmābhāve kaṭaṃ vāpi tad ūrdhve vastram āstared*{744}* //" iti [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]

[90.20] "śeṣahome 'ntahomānte āsīnau tatra carmaṇi*{745}* /
[90.21] visṛjāmi vratañ ceti tadvrataṃ carma santyajet //"*{746}* [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]

[90.22] ityādinā agnidvayasaṃsargaprakāraś ca pratipāditaḥ.

!{741}! Dieser Halbvers ist als "Gṛhya" ebenfalls zitiert in TPC 491.4. !{742}! "Gṛhya" in TPC: dvāviṃśatsaṃkhyayā. !{743}! Diese drei Halbverse sind auch als "Gṛhya" in TPC 494.13-15 zitiert. !{744}! Dieser Vers ist auch als "Gṛhya" in TPC 365.3-4 zitiert. !{745}! "Gṛhya" in TPC: śeṣahome tu homānte āsīnau tatra carmaṇi. !{746}! Dieser Vers ist als "Gṛhya" auch in TPC 401.19-20 zitiert.

[91.1] putraparigrahaprakāraś ca

[91.2] "tyāgavikrayadāneṣu prokteṣv api tatas smṛtau* /{747}*

[91.3] ekaṃ na dadyān no gṛhyāt na strī bhartrananujñayā //"*{748}* ityādinā [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]

[91.4] brahmamedhavidhis tu
[91.5] "saṃskāro brahmaniṣṭhānāṃ sadācāravatām api /
[91.6] brahmamedho 'tiphalado na sarveṣāṃ dvijanmanām //"*{749}* ityādinā [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]

[91.7] vṛṣotsargavidhis tu
[91.8] "vṛṣotsargavidhiṃ vakṣye yena pretatvamocanam /
[91.9] snātvātha vāstuhomānte pretatvasya vimuktaye* //{750}*" ityādibhiḥ [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]

[91.10] evaṃ atrānuktāni sarvāṇi gṛhyapariśiṣṭe proktāni iti veditavyam.

[91.11-15] bodhāyanādibhir apy ete sāṅgā eva pratipāditā iti cet - na. "sati kuḍye cikrakarme" ti nyāyena pradhānakarmāṇi pratipāditāni cet aṅgavicāraḥ kartavyaḥ. sandhyopāsane arghyapradānādikam anuktam. vānaprasthāśramasvīkaraṇādikam api na pratipāditam. vānaprasthāśramasvīkaraṇāsvīkaraṇāraṇyāharaṇapātralakṣaṇādiṣu vaikhānasasūtrāpekṣā asty eva. devatāpratiṣṭhādikam uktaṃ lakṣaṇam anuktam.
[91.16-18] āpastambādibhiḥ sandhyopāsanāṅkurapratisaradevatārādhanayajñopavītadhāraṇādikam apy anuktam. āpastambādīnām anyonyāpekṣā prasiddhā. anyonyāpekṣā nāma asvātantryam aṅgahīnavat.
[91.19] manu: "yad yat paravaśaṃ karma tat tad yatnena varjayet // [ManuDhŚ 4.159cd]

[91.20] sarvaṃ paravaśaṃ duḥkhaṃ sarvam ātmavaśaṃ sukham /
[91.21] etad vidyāt samāsena lakṣaṇaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ //" [ManuDhŚ 4.160]

[91.22-23] anena anantasthiraphalaprāptir darśitā. ataḥ sūtrāntaranairapekṣyāt sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ svātantryañ ca ghaṭata iti nirūpitas saptamo hetuḥ.

[91.24] iti saptamahetunirūpaṇam

!{747}! "Gṛhya" in TPC: tyāgavikriyadāneṣu yuktau svapitarau smṛtau. !{748}! Dieser Vers ist auch als "Gṛhya" in TPC 887.1-2 zitiert. !{749}! Dieser Vers ist auch zitiert als "Gṛhya" in TPC 747.18-19. !{750}! Dieser Vers ist auch zitiert als "Gṛhya" in TPC 818.20-21.

[atha aṣṭamahetunirūpaṇam]

[vaikhānasasūtrasya akhilaśiṣṭaparigṛhītatvam]

[92.1-3] idānīṃ tāvat śrutismṛtipurāṇādibhiḥ sarvottaratvenāvagatasya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya akhilaśiṣṭaparigṛhītatvam astīti darśayituṃ manvādyaiḥ svīkṛtatvād iti aṣṭamo hetuḥ nirūpyate. tathā hi

[92.5] manu: "ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmaṃ vaikhānasāśramam //"*{751}* ity ārabhya

[92.6] "puṣpamūlaphalair vāpi kevalair vartayet sadā /
[92.7] kālapakvaiḥ svayaṃ śīrṇair vaikhānasamate sthitaḥ* //{752}*" iti [ManuDhŚ 6.21]

[92.8] vyāsa: "mūlair eke phalair eke puṣpair eke dṛḍhavratāḥ / [MBh 12.236.13cd]

[92.9] vartayanti yathānyāyaṃ vaikhānasamate sthitāḥ //" iti [MBh 12.236.14ab]

[92.10] gautama: śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāyāgrāmyabhojī" iti*{753}*

[92.11] yama: śrāmaṇakena vidhānena sāyaṃ prātar upaspṛśet. iti

[92.12-13] śaṅkhalikhitau: śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāya kāle kuruvinda - veṇu - śyāmākanīvārādibhir vartayet.*{754}* iti.

[92.14-16] hārīta: vānaprastho grāmyā oṣadhī parivarjayet. tretāgnīnāṃ sthāne śrāmaṇakaṃ vāgnim ādhāya valkalaśāṇacarmakuśamuñjavidalakaṃ vā vasāno vaikhānasaproktena vidhinā vānaprastho vikhanā bhavati. anujñāyiko 'nuprasthāyikaś" ceti

[92.17] vasiṣṭha: śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāyāhitāgnir vṛkṣamūlikaḥ. iti*{755}* [VāsiṣṭhaDhŚ 9.10]

[92.18] bodhāyana: "vānaprastho vaikhānasaśāstrasamudācāraḥ" [BaudhDhS 12.6.11.14]

[92.19-21] āpastamba: "ekāgnir aniketaḥ syād"*{756}* iti. asya dharmakarpardī "gārhapatyādīnāṃ tretāgnīnāṃ sthāne yasyaiko 'gniḥ aupāsana eva - vaikhānasasūtre dṛṣṭatvāt, pāṇigrahaṇanimitvadvādaupāsanasya.

[92.22-23] jaiminīyasūtre saumikacāturmāsyaprakāraṇe. "bhāradvājapūrvaṃ yathā vaikhānasapūrvaṃ pañcaḥ" meti*{757}* (?)

!{751}! ManuDhŚ 6.1ab v.l. Dieser Halbvers ist ähnlich als "Manu" zitiert in DHN[D] 28.3. !{752}! Dieser Vers ist als "Manu" auch zitiert in DHN[D] 28.4-5. !{753}! Bezug auf GautamaDhS 1.3.26(3.27): śrāvaṇakena [śrāmaṇakena].agnim ādhāya / und auf GautamaDhS 1.3.27(3.28) agrāmyabhojī. !{754}! S.o., DHN[D] 28.10-11. !{755}! VāsiṣṭhaDhŚ: śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāyāhitāgnis syāt. !{756}! Bezug auf ĀpastambaDhS 2.9.21.20-21: tasyopadiśanti / ekāgnir aniketaḥ syād aśarmāśaraṇo muniḥ / svādhyāya evotsṛjamāno vācam. !{757}! Lies: pañcamaḥ" iti.

[akhilaśiṣṭaparigrahasya prāmāṇyātiśayahetutvam]

[93.1-2] atrobhayatra ātrivyākhyānam - ṣoḍaśartvijāṃ madhye bhāradvājasūtriṇaṃ prastotāraṃ vaikhānasasūtriṇaṃ pratihartāraṃ varayet" iti.

[93.6] āśrame vā vane vā 'pi putradārasamāhitaḥ /
[93.7] aṣṭākṣaraparo nityaṃ sa vaikhānasa ucyate* //{759}* [KapiñjalaS]

[93.8] grāmyadharmāṇi sarvāṇi varjayed vanavāsakaḥ*{760}* /

[93.12] vane vā pattane vāpi japed vaikhānasaḥ śuciḥ //

[93.14] anyair api evam evoktam.

[93.15-16] akhilaśiṣṭaparigrahe ko viśeṣa iti cet - akhilaśiṣṭaparigrahāt prāmāṇyātiśayo 'stīty avagamyate.
